Guo's Troops Capture Longgang 80

▲ He Chengjun Immediately Departs to Supervise the Troops

▲ Bandit Leader Xie Hanxun of Central Hubei Handed Over for Trial

Hankou dispatch: The various bands of Red bandits in Hubei Province have been routed by the National Army advancing on multiple fronts. Over the course of several months, all important towns have been successively recovered. Only the isolated area of Longgang in southern Hubei remains in the hands of the bandits. This area belongs to Yangxin County and, like Yanxia, is an old stronghold of Kong Long's bandit gang. Surrounded by high mountains and blocked by small rivers, it is strategically important. The bandits have been entrenched there for six years. The county borders Jiangxi and provides easy access to Hunan, allowing the bandits to flee and reappear at will. This has become their common tactic. This time, the National Army launched a large-scale bandit suppression campaign. Because of the power of He Long and Kuang Jixun's factions, heavy troops were dispatched to annihilate their main forces. On the southern Hubei front, Guo Runian, Zhang Gang, Rong Jingfang, and other units advanced to suppress the bandits. Since May, they have successively recovered Yinzu, Liurenba, Tongcheng, and other places. A month ago, Minister He Yingqin convened a bandit suppression conference in Nanchang with the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, dividing troops to block and suppress the bandits on multiple fronts. After recovering Sanxikou, the remaining bandits suffered heavy losses and were cut off from communication. One group fled to the border area between Wanzai and Liuyang, while another group fled into the old stronghold of Longgang. Guo, Zhang, and other units launched a continuous campaign towards Longgang. Because the bandits defended the river, they could not advance directly. On the morning of the 2nd of this month, Division Commander Guo Runian personally led the 26th Division, erected pontoon bridges, and crossed the river under the cover of machine guns. The bandits fired fiercely from across the river. The officers and soldiers bravely advanced, crossed the river through a hail of bullets, occupied the position, and dispersed the bandits. In the afternoon, the unit searched and advanced towards Luojia Ferry, discovering more than 1,000 Red bandits in the mountain flanks on both sides. They resisted stubbornly, but were encircled and annihilated. The bandits in Longgang, relying on the bandit troops defending the front and the treacherous mountains and forests, were unprepared. That night, Commander Guo dispatched troops to attack Longgang. The dispatched unit, the 76th Brigade, consisting of about four battalions, was led by Brigade Commander Huang Hanxun and set out at 2:00 AM on the 3rd, traveling quickly and lightly. They soon arrived at the location. The bandits, caught off guard, fought desperately in hand-to-hand combat for several hours. By 11:00 AM, the bandits could no longer hold out and fled to Yanxia. At 12:00 PM, Guo's troops completely occupied Longgang. Both sides fought with their main forces in this battle, and many bandits were killed. Even more were captured after the occupation. The troops are now joining forces with friendly forces to advance towards Yanxia, with plans to capture it on the 4th. The group that fled to Liuyang and Wanzai will be dealt with by the Hunan Army. It was previously said that He Chengjun would personally go to southern Hubei to supervise the suppression of Kong's bandits. Although the bandits have been defeated, the remnants still need to be cleared. It is said that he will depart in the next few days to supervise the pursuit and annihilation of the bandits, ensuring that they are completely wiped out. However, the administrative office may cease its organization. In the eastern Hubei area, since the recovery of Jinjiazhai, the bandits have been completely defeated. Recently, they regrouped the remnants and fled west from Yingshan on the 2nd. Division Commander Hao Mengling discovered this and ambushed them in the eastern and western areas of Tuanpo. Taking advantage of the bandits' hasty retreat, they launched a surprise attack from the intersections of Lukou, Dajiaji, and Luotuo Ao, cutting them into several sections and killing more than 1,000. Even more were captured. In addition, Commander Tang Enbo searched and suppressed bandits in Pengda Bay, Hejia House, Longjia House, Gaoshan, and other areas. In Pengda Bay, they defeated 7,000 to 8,000 remnant bandits. According to captured bandits, Longjia House was occupied by the pseudo-Macheng Independent Division. They immediately advanced towards the village and surrounded it. More than 400 Red bandits resisted stubbornly but were ultimately eliminated. More than 100 Mauser and infantry rifles were seized, and more than 300 bandits were captured. The eastern Hubei area has been largely cleared. However, when Jinjiazhai was recovered, the remaining bandits fled in disarray. It is feared that a few scattered bandits may have fled to various places, hoping to revive their cause. On the 3rd, it was rumored that bandits had been discovered in the Huanggang area. The authorities have dispatched troops to suppress them. The Second Fleet of the Navy has also dispatched the Weisheng warship from Wuhan to cruise the Tuanfeng and Huangshigang areas to assist the army in blocking and suppressing the bandits.

In the central Hubei area, it was rumored that He's bandits were in Yichang. In reality, they have indeed fled to Yangping, which belongs to Yuan'an County. This area has been repeatedly harassed by He's bandits. In addition to the National Army's advancing units, including Liu Maoen, Xiao Zhichu, and Fan Shisheng's units, which have established a tight encirclement on three sides, the Sichuan Army's Guo Xun, Zhang Bangben, and Fan Shaozeng's units are also following and pursuing on multiple routes. They are currently in a tight encirclement and will be resolved soon. Wang Yiming's bandit unit and the pseudo-independent regiment still have more than 2,000 men. One night, they fled from Sunqiao to Longdang, hoping to join forces with He's bandits. Xiao's division, together with Yu Zhaolong's brigade and Zhang and Li's regiments, pursued and suppressed them. Fu's regiment ambushed and blocked them at Guanqiao. Zhang and Li's regiments pursued them to Sanyangdian on the 2nd and launched a pincer attack, annihilating most of them. The remaining bandits continue to flee north and are being pursued vigorously. The Honghu area has been declared clear. The National Army has successively seized more than 7,000 Mauser and infantry rifles, more than 60 machine guns, and more than 30 mortars. All important leaders have been captured. With the exception of Lu Yi, who was executed on the spot with the approval of Xu Yuanquan's headquarters at the request of the people, the rest were escorted from Xindi to Wuhan on the evening of the 2nd by Liu Ao, the chief of the military law office, for detailed interrogation. They include: Ma Wu, the second chairman of the pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-West Provincial Soviet and director of the Political Security Bureau; Zhou Meitong, the chairman of the pseudo-Provincial Soviet; Wang Wensuan (female), the secretary of the pseudo-Women's Department; Zhao Zunyi (female), the secretary and teacher of the pseudo-Lenin School (wife of Zhu Mianzhi, an important Communist Party member); Li Yezhong (female), the secretary of the pseudo-Lenin School (wife of Liu Luoxia, an important Communist Party member); Zhang Shenming, the political secretary and military doctor of the first hospital of the pseudo-hospital special branch committee independent regiment medical office political department; Zhang Huichuan, the secretary of the special service regiment of the pseudo-7th Division; Zhu Xianzai, the traffic officer of the pseudo-Fu County district; Peng Mingdeng, the propaganda officer of the pseudo-County Committee; Lei Ziquan, the propaganda officer of the pseudo-County Government; Peng Zhifa, the handyman of the pseudo-Provincial Committee; Hu Shaomin, a staff member of the radio station and Red Flag newspaper; Duan Yuheng, Duan Dechang's paternal uncle; Duan Liujin and Duan Qijin, paternal cousins; Duan Yongshi, Duan's grandmother (over 70 years old); Duan's aunt; Duan Wuxian, Duan's younger sister; Duan Chuanzhi, Duan's young daughter (child); Hong Juzun, Duan's divorced wife; and Meng Guirong, Duan Liujin's wife. They are all currently under interrogation in Wuhan. (October 3rd)

Dredging the Huai River and Opening Waterways to the Yangtze River 81

▲ Constructing Three Dams for Easy Opening and Closing

▲ Proposing to Issue 9 Million Yuan in Public Bonds

Zhenjiang dispatch: The Huai River diversion project has been underway for more than a month since resuming on September 1st. According to the revised plan for splitting and diverting the river into the sea and the Yangtze River this summer, both the sea and Yangtze River routes should be undertaken simultaneously. However, due to insufficient funding and labor shortages, the work in the past month has focused on dredging the section from Lianshui County to the sea, the waterway to the Yangtze River has not been considered yet. Currently, because the first step of the flood discharge project is an urgent and crucial task, the Huai River Diversion Committee has converted 9,000 tons of disaster relief wheat allocated by the National Government last year into 300,000 yuan in cash from the Ministry of Finance. This money will be used to hire an additional 3,000 workers to dredge the waterway to the Yangtze River, continuing the work-for-relief method. The committee has already recruited 2,000 workers from Bengbu and Wuhu in Anhui Province. The remaining workers will be recruited locally. As for the Yangtze River project plan, it has been decided to first discharge the excess water from Hongze Lake into the Zhangfu diversion river to enter the canal. Two branches of the tailwater will be opened in the southeast of Hongze Lake to enter the Gaobao and other lakes. New-style movable dams will be built at the junctions of the Zhangfu diversion river and the two branches of Hongze Lake. When the lake water is high, the dams will be opened for discharge; when the lake water is low, the dams will be closed for storage. This will benefit the originally planned first step of flood discharge, second step of irrigation, and third step of navigation. The Qingjiangpu Works Bureau operated a Huai River Diversion Training Class in Pu in 1928 to train junior technical personnel for the Huai River diversion into the sea. The training lasted six months and achieved good results. The Works Bureau also plans to follow the previous example, but with an emphasis on the Yangtze River direction. The bureau is now actively preparing and aims to establish the class within the shortest possible time. However, the Yangtze River water system is very complex. Although the initial dredging project has begun, the downstream waterways still need to be carefully surveyed. Twenty-two engineers from the bureau organized a survey team on September 27th, divided into hydrology, surveying and mapping, and geology groups. They departed on September 30th to the Gaobao Lake area to conduct surveying and mapping and drilling to test the soil quality. However, the newly excavated river channels for both the Yangtze River and the sea require the purchase of 120,000 mu of farmland. The Huai River Diversion Committee has also established a land administration bureau within the Qingjiang Works Bureau to carry out land acquisition. The second batch of tools ordered from the United Kingdom arrived in China in mid-September and have now all arrived in Pu. It is said that this batch of tools is worth about 3 million yuan, which has been deducted from the Boxer Indemnity water fees by the Ministry of Finance. The Huai River Diversion Committee believes that since the Yangtze River project has now begun, funding must be secured in order to achieve complete success. The first phase of the project this year requires 16 million yuan, but it is difficult to allocate this amount at a time when the government's finances are exhausted. However, at least 9 million yuan is needed to maintain operations, so the committee has petitioned the National Government to approve the issuance of 9 million yuan in public bonds to meet the needs.

Supreme Court Denies Southwestern Branch 82

The Supreme Court today informed Lu Sihui, the President of the Guangdong High Court, that: The Supreme Court received Instructed Word No. 160 from the Judicial Yuan on September 29th, stating that: "Upon reviewing the Southwest Political Affairs Committee's consultation and report on the resolution to establish a Southwestern Branch of the Supreme Court, the court has already responded, requesting that the resolution be revoked and informing the court on file. Now, according to Lu Sihui's report, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee has appointed him to concurrently manage the administrative affairs of the Southwestern Branch of the Supreme Court, and he is following the organization's establishment. The establishment of a branch has not been approved by the court, so how can it be established on its own? Any judgment made by this illegal organization is naturally deemed invalid. In addition to consulting the Southwest Political Affairs Committee again to quickly revoke the branch, the Ministry of Justice must also be informed to instruct the high courts of the Southwest provinces to comply." Upon review, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee's resolution to organize a southwestern branch of the Supreme Court lacks a basis in both law and reason, and will only create disputes. It has already been submitted to the Judicial Yuan for review based on law and fact and rejected in detail. The Judicial Yuan and the Ministry of Justice have successively consulted and rejected the request to quickly cancel the illegal organizational resolution in order to avoid disrupting the judicial system and maintain the spirit of unity. Now, according to the report, it has been organized and established on its own, which is extremely inappropriate. According to the court's organization, there is a statutory system, and it cannot be disrupted at will. Since the law has been established, the entire country should jointly maintain it. Moreover, those who hold judicial responsibilities should be especially careful to abide by and set an example for the masses, so that the rule of law can be achieved. An illegal organization like this has no basis of its own, and yet it wants to execute judgments and hear grievances. How can it be believed by the people? In order to maintain the rule of law and the unified judicial system, the court must abide by the instructions of the Judicial Yuan. The establishment of the branch as presented is not approved. Any judgment made by this illegal organization is naturally deemed invalid according to law. In addition to the Judicial Yuan consulting the Southwest Political Affairs Committee again to quickly revoke the branch, the Ministry of Justice must also be informed to instruct the high courts of the Southwest provinces to comply.

Journey to the West (3)(10)(2) 83

As Long as Heaven Rains

At four or five o'clock in the afternoon of the tenth, three or five of us went out of the west gate of Hancheng for a suburban tour. We saw that the crops in the fields, such as corn and millet, were very flourishing, which made us often feel that the suffering endured by the people of Shaanxi over the years was not entirely due to natural shortcomings, but suffered great losses in terms of human affairs. The countryside has been completely bankrupt, and most of the harvest that farmers painstakingly obtain in the fields every year is not enough to pay the various taxes. Therefore, they no longer want to farm and flee to various places.

"Are your village chiefs good?" we asked a farmer carrying a hoe and about to return home while walking.

"Alas, there are many bad ones, but there are also those with conscience," the old farmer replied with a sigh.

"Why don't you sue the bad village chiefs?" we asked the old farmer sincerely again.

"We have no money and don't know anyone, who dares to sue him?" the old farmer replied again.

"Now, do you have any difficulties or painful things? Please tell us honestly," we asked again.

"As long as Heaven rains, no matter how much money the officials want, we are willing to give it. Other than that, we have no more difficulties,"

The old farmer told us very sadly and thoughtfully.

"Is your current county magistrate good? How does he treat the common people?" we asked him again.

"Oh, I dare not say. He is the parents of the common people, I dare not criticize him," the old farmer replied hesitantly.

After listening to the old farmer's few words, we all sighed to each other, "The Chinese people are really good people, but..." In this way, we walked listlessly for more than ten minutes and then approached the dormitory. After dinner, representatives from all walks of life in the local area met with us and provided us with some general information about Hancheng.

Hancheng was once the ancient state of Han and the state of Liang. In the Spring and Autumn period, it was called Hanyuan. The states of Qin and Jin once met here in battle. In the eleventh year of Qin Huiwen, it was renamed Xiayang. Wang Mang of the Han Dynasty changed it to Pseudo-Ji Pavilion. It belonged to Huashan Commandery in the Jin Dynasty. Hancheng County was established in the Qing Dynasty. At the beginning of the Tang Dynasty, the prefecture and county were abolished. At the end of the Tang Dynasty, it was renamed Hanyuan. After the Five Dynasties, the Later Tang restored Hanyuan to Hancheng, which belonged to Tongzhou. The Jin Dynasty considered it Zhen Prefecture, but the Yuan Dynasty abolished it and assigned it to Tongzhou. The Ming Dynasty followed this. In the third year of Yongzheng in the Qing Dynasty, it was changed to a directly governed prefecture. In the thirteenth year, it was promoted to a prefecture. Now it is Hancheng County. There are many places of scenic beauty and historical sites. Liangshan is ninety li northwest of the county, stretching east and west. The shape of the arch is like a roof beam. There is a stone pagoda, a Luohan cave, and a spring called Tianjing and Longjing. There are also east and west valleys. Longmen Mountain is sixty li northeast of the county and was dug by Yu to connect the Mengjin River estuary. It is eighty paces wide, with traces of chiseling on the edge of the cliff, and the legacy of his work still remains. The water of the Yellow River flows down from the top of the mountain like boiling and surging, as fast as a bamboo arrow, and four horses cannot catch up. The west cliffs are all broken mountains and cliffs. Fish gather under Longmen, but thousands cannot ascend. According to legend, only the divine dragon can cross, hence the name. The Two Stone Treasures are at the foot of Sanlei Mountain, where hermits live. The South Stone Treasure of the side creek is beside the creek water. Elephant Mountain is twenty li west of the county. The mountain rises and falls like an elephant drinking from a pool. Hengshan is twenty li northwest of the county. The mountain stones are uniquely beautiful, and there is a stone cave where the Daoist Second Hejing Yuan ascended to heaven. Five Zhi Mountain is in the middle of Wanshan, with deep rocks and distant valleys, rarely visited by humans. There are east, west, north, south, and middle five zhi. The mountain has many pine trees and spring water. Susuan Ancient Trail is winding and tortuous, the location of the tomb of Su Wu of the Pseudo-Han Dynasty. In addition, there are the Phoenix Mountain, Xiangshan Mountain, Peony Mountain, Ape Mountain, Lion Ridge Mountain, Horse Head Mountain, Shendao Ridge, MaRidge, Zhu Sha Ridge, Wenjia Ridge, Bailin Cave, and Niuxin Gorge, all of which are very famous. The largest waters are the Yellow River, fifteen li east of the county, flowing in from Yichuan. The Gushui River is hundreds of li north of the county, the Jushui River is one li southwest of the county, the Taoqu River is more than ten li northwest of the county, the Huachi Pool is seventeen li southwest of the county, and the Wenshui River is twenty li north of the county. Canal administration has been extremely emphasized since ancient times, and thousands of good fields rely on it for irrigation.

Hancheng County covers an area of ​​about one hundred li from east to west and about one hundred and ten li from north to south. There are the magical traces of Yu Gate, the fragrant grass of the Han Shrine, the dark color of Su Cen, the high tomb of the Grand Historian, the ancient road of Hanyuan, the wild geese of the Great Wall Fortress, the willows of the embankment of Shaoliang, the afterglow of Gaomen, the cloud temple of Xiangshan, the sparse mirror of Yuanjue, the misty rain of Hengshan, and the twelve scenes of Zuoyuan Tanghua. In addition, there are the Shenyu Temple, Zixia Temple, Houtu Temple, Chen Ping Temple, Grand Historian's Temple, Su Wu Temple, Guo Ziyi Temple, Eight Immortals Cave, Laozi Cave, Leishen Cave, and Sima Slope.

Page 8

However, due to time constraints, they cannot be written out one by one.

The county has 16,000 households, with a population of more than 92,000 people. There are more than 1,130 households in the city and near suburbs, with a population of more than 10,000 people. The people's lives are very simple, and each person needs about four or five yuan a month to survive. The city is square, with each side about three li long. There are about 170 shops in the city. The total tax revenue of the county in a year is about 108,000 yuan. The temporary special appropriation is about 200,000 yuan per year. In addition, there are contract registration tax and tobacco tax. The total amount of various fees paid by the people in a year is about 500,000 yuan.

There is one junior high school and three complete elementary schools (one for girls, one vocational, and one general) in the city. There are two complete elementary schools outside the city and about 170 or 180 primary schools. The middle school has about 160 students, the complete elementary schools have about 380 students, and the primary schools have about 6,000 students. The educational expenses are about 2,300 yuan per year from land rent and house rent, about 3,200 yuan per year from miscellaneous taxes, and about 14,000 yuan per year from the financial bureau. The distribution method is about 6,000 yuan per year for middle schools, about 9,000 yuan per year for complete elementary schools, and primary schools are borne by the villagers themselves. The educational administration expenses are about 2,000 yuan per year. The salaries of teachers and staff are 30 yuan per month for the middle school principal, 15 yuan for the director, 5 jiao per hour for the teachers, 24 yuan for the elementary school principal, and about 20 yuan for the teachers. Except for the middle school teaching English for five hours per week per grade and the elementary school for one hour of English, the courses are the same as other schools. Folk schools have been suspended since the famine and have not yet been restored. The director of the Education Bureau had a student strike in May and was driven away, and has not yet been officially appointed. Other situations are omitted due to time constraints.

Investigation of Hancheng Coal Mine, Etc. 84

Before 9:00 PM on the eleventh, the members of the delegation who investigated the Hancheng Coal Mine and the Longmen Water Conservancy returned one after another. The coal mine team arrived at Shijia Gully at 11:00 AM on the tenth, and arrived at Quanzi Gully at 8:00 PM. There was gas in the mine, and because they were not prepared, the gas almost ignited when it touched the light, and their lives were almost lost. On the eleventh, the investigation of the Qiaoer Gully and Xigou two coal mines were in good condition. The investigation of the Hancheng coal field is as follows:

The Hancheng coalfield has good quality and a flat seam, bordering the Yellow River in the east, making it a place of great interest to mining surveyors. The investigation is described as follows:

(1) Shijia Gully Coal Mine. The mine is located 18 li north of Hancheng County. Coal is extracted using an inclined shaft, which is three and a half feet high and four feet wide. The mine tunnel is winding and generally opens to the northwest, with an inclination of 20 to 40 degrees and a straight depth of about 40 zhang. The coal seam is about one and a half feet thick, trending north-northwest to south-southeast,

Inclined to the southwest. Each worker can mine 600 to 1,000 jin of coal per shift. The wage is about 4 jiao per person per day, or 150 copper coins per worker (the exchange rate is 400 coins per yuan). Each puller can pull eight times a day, each time pulling about 40 or 50 jin. The wage is about 4 jiao. Food and lamp oil are provided by the workers themselves. Each person uses about 6 liang of oil per shift, costing 1 jiao and 2 or 3 fen. The price of coal sold at the mine is 1 jiao and 5 fen per dou (80 jin), or about 3 yuan and 2 jiao per ton.

▲Errata: The above paragraphs should be above Journey to the West (31) in yesterday's newspaper. Due to an error in page layout, it is corrected here.

Resistance is the Only Way to Survive 85

On the way back, the water conservancy team was told a recent story by villagers: Previously, bandits in the suburbs ran rampant everywhere, extorting money and kidnapping people, which was very vicious. So the rich fled and the poor waited for death. In the end, the people could no longer bear it, so they made hundreds of red-tasseled iron spears and resisted the bandits with all their might. As a result, they killed more than 200 bandits in the first battle, and the bandit scourge has since disappeared. Alas, resistance, resistance, is the only bright path for us to survive!

Originally, our return journey was supposed to go from Dali to Sanyuan and then to Xi'an, and then report to Huashan from Xi'an. Looking at the map, we circled a huge elliptical circle, and many people thought that,

This way of walking is not cost-effective in terms of time, energy, and economy. Therefore, on the evening of the eleventh, we all decided to report directly to Huashan from Dali. After the report is completed in four or five days, people with free time can wander around Xi'an for a few days, and people who are busy with official business can take the train that has not been seen for more than a month, as fast as a hurricane, and return to their sweet hometown. (Sent from Hancheng on September 12)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 86

▲Provincial Order to Investigate Rice Production. The rice harvest in various villages and towns this year is still considered abundant, so the rice market is gradually falling. Now, at the time of the early rice harvest, the price per stone is 7 or 8 yuan. In the future, the late rice harvest will be no more than 6 or 7 yuan. Low grain prices hurt farmers, which is of great importance to the rural economy. Moreover, recently, the domestic rice market has been manipulated by foreign markets, and the harvest in Hangzhou and Shaoxing this year has been poor. The province is restricted by the order prohibiting exports and cannot adjust the surplus. Now, Zhu Yuanzhi, chairman of the Songjiang County Chamber of Commerce, has submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs, asking them to consider the hardships of the people and allow the ban on rice exports to be lifted in order to maintain the hardships of farmers, etc. The Songjiang County Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county government to report on the harvest and market conditions this year, as well as the surplus or deficit situation in the past year, for review and decision.

▲Extension of the Land Price Tax Deadline. The deadline for the first installment of the land price tax was set for the end of September by the provincial order, and late payment fines would be levied. The announcement is on file. Now, various institutions such as Kuangchan are requesting a one-month extension to ease the tax burden and increase tax revenue. The County Finance Bureau has specially ordered both to continue collecting the first installment of the land price tax before receiving the department order.

Fengxian 87

▲Clearing Overdue Land Tax. The overdue land tax in this county has been a long-standing issue. Various institutions and local gentry have organized clearing committees to carry out clearing work. At the last local administrative meeting, local gentry Ruan Xiyao and others were again elected as clearing committee members to organize a clearing committee to hire accountants to carry out active clearing. After several months of accounting, the accounts for the eighteenth, nineteenth, and twentieth years have been completely cleared. It is heard that the accumulated provincial and local taxes for the three years amount to a total of 192,562 yuan, 1 jiao, and 0.09 li. Now the committee is engaged in clearing the work before the eighteenth year. In addition, the committee's clearing of overdue land tax this time is extremely precise. After many inquiries and verifications, the amount of land in the county is also very clear. It is heard that the total amount of taxed land in the county is 528,830 mu, 5 fen, 9 li, and 6 hao. Except for old wasteland, public occupation, collapsed land, roads, and unclaimed debts, the total amount of ripe land actually collected in the county is 518,412 mu, 8 fen, 3 li, and 9 hao. This time, the committee members calculated the above-mentioned overdue debts based on the actual amount of ripe land collected. However, it is heard that there is no way to check the old wasteland, public occupation, and collapsed land in the archives of the County Finance Bureau.

Suzhou 88

▲Agreement Reached on Borrowing Education Funds. Because the Provincial Education Funds Management Office owed a large amount of education funds in the 20th year, it telegraphed Zhu Yuankai, the Suzhou Commissioner, to work with the county government to borrow 80,000 yuan from the banking and money industries, using the second installment of the land price tax education surcharge for this year as collateral, to be repaid in four months, with a monthly interest rate of 1.4%. It is heard that an agreement has now been reached after Zhu's handling, and the funds will be turned over in the near future.

▲Digging Up Ancient Tombs. The ancient tomb of a Yuan Dynasty Daoist Wang in Qingzhouguanqian Guangrenli in the city was excavated. The second branch of the Public Security Bureau has detained the foreman Shi Ruchun and transferred the case to the local court for review on the 4th.

Wuxi 89

▲ Request to Postpone the Implementation of the New Weights and Measures: The County Government previously received an instruction from the Department of Industry, requiring all counties in Jiangsu Province to implement the new weights and measures by the end of this year. Tang Fuqian was appointed as the county's weights and measures inspector and has been actively carrying out various plans since taking office. He stipulated that starting from the first day of this month, the reforms would begin with vegetable market vendors. Prior notice was given to each public security sub-bureau to dispatch police to assist. In the past few days, the results have been excellent, with all vendors having replaced their scales with new ones. However, Mr. Tang believes that other industries also urgently need to be reformed, so it is decided that starting from the 15th, industries such as tea, lacquer, medicine, wax candles, and coal and iron will also be reformed. Yesterday, separate letters were sent to each trade association, forwarding them to member businesses, urging them to promptly order new scales and use them as scheduled. However, the county chamber of commerce believes that in this time of social and economic decline and difficult living conditions, using the new scales, which are only 80% of the commonly used scale codes, is tantamount to raising the prices of all goods in society. Reports from Shanghai and Jiangsu indicate that requests have been made to postpone the implementation. Therefore, a letter has been sent to the county government requesting a postponement to avoid unrest.

▲ Night Boat Robbery: A night boat from this county to Jintong Bridge Town in Jiangyin was carrying more than 30 passengers and goods the other night. As usual, it set off from Wuxi. However, when it entered the Baitang Weikou area, it was already past 10 p.m., and a pirate ship suddenly appeared. Eight or nine bandits jumped out, each wielding weapons. They fired a shot into the air first, yelling for the boat to stop. After boarding the boat, they looted at will for about an hour, taking away silver, goods, and passengers' clothing, worth about five or six hundred yuan. Afterward, the boat owner issued a loss report, reported it to the shipping association, and forwarded it to the county government, requesting the arrest of the thieves.

Zhenjiang 90

▲ Departure of the Provincial Land Bureau Survey Team: The internal affairs of the Provincial Land Bureau have now been sorted out, and the county magistrates of Danyang and 19 other counties have been appointed as members of the Land Bureau Preparatory Committee. It is now learned that the bureau has also dispatched the third surveying team to Zhenjiang and the fourth surveying team to Jiangning and Guangde to continue handling the land survey. The third and fourth groups of the map base team have gone to Qingpu and Fengxian to start surveying the county map base points, and they have all departed on time. It is also heard that other teams will be dispatched to Danyang, Yixing, and Liyang counties to begin surveying and measuring, so the bureau's work has been quite tense recently.

▲ Gradual Rise in Silk Prices: The purchase prices of silk in Zhenjiang are several yuan higher than a week ago. Due to the scarcity of supply and excessive demand, silk merchants have no choice but to raise the purchase prices in order to obtain substantial profits when selling. The recent prices are compared with the prices a week ago as follows: Recent prices: First grade: 35 yuan per 100 taels; Second grade: 33 yuan; Third grade: 31 yuan; Fourth grade: 28 yuan. Prices a week ago: First grade: 32 yuan; Second grade: 30 yuan; Third grade: 28 yuan; Fourth grade: 26 yuan.

Yangzhou 91

▲ Bandit Robbery of Run Chang Bank: At 3 a.m. on the third, several bandits suddenly entered the Run Chang Bank inside the De Da Oil Shop on Jiangjiaqiao Street, breaking straight into the silver room and looting more than 1,600 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars. They also shot and wounded the person in charge of the silver room and escaped with the loot. Jingjiang 92

▲ Jiang Yu Steamer Collides with Naval Survey Ship: The Jiang Yu steamer was launched on the second and was unloading passengers outside the Bawei Port at 11 p.m. At that time, a naval survey ship was moored there. The driver of the Jiang Yu steamer did not pay attention and suddenly crashed the bow of the ship into the survey ship, sinking quite deeply. Fortunately, it did not leak. The Jiang Yu steamer also suffered minor damage. The captain of the survey ship and the owner of the Jiang Yu steamer both signed an agreement. The Jiang Yu steamer continued to sail as usual, while the survey ship was still moored in the river. It is heard that the machinery has been damaged and cannot move.

Nantong 93

▲ Handover Issues of the Water Police District Chief: Jiang Chaoxiong, the chief of the Fourth Water Police District of Jiangsu Province, was dismissed due to a case and detained by the Provincial Public Security Bureau in the provincial capital for unclear handover. The two largest items in the handover were the shortage of firearms and the issuance of police salaries. Jiang said that the firearms were lost when the district headquarters was located in Wusong when the Shanghai Incident suddenly occurred, and it was impossible to retrieve them. Regarding the salary account, a representative, Li Kai, was sent to Nantong on the 3rd to reconcile the accounts with the new district chief, Zhang Xianyi. Zhang Dong, a provincial commissioner, supervised the reconciliation.

▲ Tax Police Stationed in Nantong Head to Haizhou: More than 1,000 tax police from the Ministry of Finance stationed in Nantong, led by Nan Shan, have been ordered to go to Haizhou to suppress bandits and protect taxes.

Gaoyou 94

▲ Kidnapping and Robbery Incident in Shajia Weir: Hu Bicheng, a grain merchant from Shajia Weir in the eighth district of the county, was transporting a boatload of soybeans the other day when he encountered more than a dozen bandits. He was robbed of more than 200 yuan in cash. Before leaving, the bandits kidnapped Hu's youngest son, fired a shot into the air, and fled.

Jiaxing 95

▲ Postponement of Contract Tax and Land Tax Penalties: Jiaxing's contract tax was ordered by the province to be paid by the end of September, and penalties would be imposed after the deadline. It is learned that the Department of Finance, in order to show compassion for the people, has telegraphed the county to postpone the penalties for three months starting in October. In addition, the upper period land tax for the 21st year was originally scheduled to be penalized starting on October 1st, but the Finance Bureau has presented a request to the Department of Finance to postpone it until November 1st. In addition, the official property investigation office has already completed its work, but there is still official property that has not been fully processed, and people's reports of encroachment and occupation are still pouring in. Therefore, a telegram has been sent to the Department of Finance requesting instructions and approval to extend the deadline for one month.

Huzhou 96

▲ Kidnappers Kill Hostage: Xu Ziquan, from Shanglin Village, Dongcun, near Yacun in the northeastern part of Huzhou, was known to be a well-off family. In December of last year, he was suddenly kidnapped by Huzhou bandits. A letter was sent demanding a large ransom. Xu Zimeisheng raised 5,000 yuan and took it to the Jiangsu border to redeem his father. However, Xu Ziquan had already been killed by the bandits. On the night of September 30th of this year, another pirate ship arrived with a dozen bandits, each carrying wooden-cased guns. They landed and suddenly went to Xu's house, kidnapped Xu Meisheng, took him onto the ship, and left.

Hangzhou 97

▲ Appeal Judgment in Sheng Xuanhuai's Daughter's Divorce Case: The sixth daughter of Sheng Xuanhuai (Xingsun) of Wujin, known in Shanghai as Miss Sheng Liu, is 38 years old. In the second year of the Xuantong era of the Qing Dynasty, she was betrothed to Liu Yanting, the son of Liu Tiqing, a wealthy man from Nanxun. They married in the first year of the Republic, and the couple got along quite well. They had two daughters, Zhenbao and Qingbao. In the sixth year of the Republic, Miss Sheng and her husband turned against each other and returned to Ningbo. In the 18th year of the Republic, she filed a lawsuit with the Wuxing branch of the Hangzhou County District Court seeking a divorce from her husband, demanding 350,000 taels of alimony, the return of 94,640 yuan in dowry money, and the repayment of 150,000 taels in alimony loans and 50,000 taels in educational expenses for the two daughters. The branch court ruled on July 25, 20th year of the Republic, granting the divorce and ordering the defendant to repay the plaintiff, Liu Sheng, 52,200 yuan in alimony before the divorce and to refund 10,000 yuan in dowry expenses to Miss Sheng. Subsequently, both parties were dissatisfied and appealed to the High Court in Hangzhou. Each time they submitted a complaint, the stamp duty alone amounted to several thousand yuan. The results of the trial have now been announced. Yesterday, the appeal of both parties was rejected, and the original judgment was upheld. However, it is heard that Liu Yanting had already taken a concubine and had a son in the sixth year of the Republic, and Miss Sheng also has a new love, a Peking opera actor named Zhao Junyu, and a child has recently been born. Therefore, after mediation by others, the plaintiff and defendant have hopes of reaching a settlement.

▲ Rebels on the Zhejiang Border Allowed to Reintegrate: The three counties of Jiangshan, Changshan, and Kaihua on the Zhejiang border are located on the border of Fujian and Jiangxi provinces, and have been repeatedly harassed by Red bandits. Many ordinary people in the counties have inevitably been coerced by the bandits. Recently, due to the large-scale encirclement and suppression, the bandits have been forced to flee into the mountains, and the coerced people dare not return to their homeland and are displaced, which is pitiful. The provincial government believes that these people did not willingly join the bandits and were repeatedly threatened by them, which is understandable. Therefore, a method for allowing them to reintegrate has been drafted, ordering them to surrender to the respective county governments, write a letter of repentance, and have the local village chief and clan leader issue a guarantee, proving that they have genuinely repented. They will then be allowed to reintegrate and will not be prosecuted.

Commissioner Zhao then departed from Hangzhou and went directly to Sheng County to supervise the suppression of bandits. It is now learned that Commissioner Zhao believes that the bandits in the three counties of Xinchang, Shengxian, and Fenghua have formed mobile bandits. If they are not wiped out as soon as possible, they may become a major problem. Therefore, he convened a bandit suppression conference with the magistrates of six counties, including Xinchang, Shengxian, Fenghua, Yinxian, Yuyao, and Xia, to discuss methods for suppressing the bandits and carrying out rural cleanup. The other night, he sent a special telegram to Secretary Mou Xiaotian in the Ningbo office, informing the magistrate of Yinxian County to go to Sheng County to discuss the matter as soon as possible. The magistrate of Yinxian County, Chen Baolin, obeyed the order and took the early train to Sheng County this morning (the 3rd).

He paid courtesy calls to various important agencies that day (the 3rd). He declined all social gatherings. After a short stay in Bengbu, he went to various counties to inspect.

Special Report

A Humble Opinion on Reforming China's School Education 102

(6) Cheng Tianfang

Now, let's give some examples to illustrate. If Province A is building a certain number of miles of highway, and after the highway is completed, a certain number of people will definitely be needed to drive public buses, then the vocational school in Province A should open a bus driver training class to train these bus drivers. It should recruit students who have graduated from elementary school and are above a certain age, and provide them with six months of training so that they can drive buses, repair buses, roughly understand the principles of bus construction, and know various laws regarding highways and driving buses. After six months, they should pass an examination and be issued a license before they can become bus drivers. Wouldn't bus drivers trained in this way be better than bus drivers recruited casually? In this way, on the one hand, the individual's livelihood problem can be solved, and at the same time, because there are good drivers, public safety will be better guaranteed. For example, Province B is a silk-producing area. To develop the silk industry and improve silkworm breeds and silkworm rearing methods, a group of people is needed to do these things. The vocational school in Province B should open a silkworm silk class, recruiting students who have graduated from elementary school and are above a certain age, and provide them with one year or one and a half years of training so that they know how to select silkworm breeds, how to arrange silkworm houses, and how to improve silkworm rearing and silk reeling methods, not only knowing but also practicing. After completing the course, they should pass an examination and be issued a license, or they can go to engage in improving silkworm silk production themselves, or they can be appointed by the government to various counties to guide people in improving the silkworm silk industry. In this way, the individual's livelihood problem can also be solved, and at the same time, social productivity will benefit.

The above are just a few examples. In addition, we can infer that vocational schools must be run in this way to adapt to the needs of society and increase social productivity. The more vocational schools of this kind, the better, because society needs that kind of person, so it opens that kind of class. Once the needs of society have been met, it can stop running that kind of class at any time. Naturally, all students who come out of vocational schools can use what they have learned to support themselves. I advocate that vocational schools should not charge tuition fees and should set up more scholarships or loan amounts to reward students from poor families who work hard to study. Because the students in vocational schools are mostly children from poor families, the country should help them become productive members within the scope of its possibilities.

There are also many occupations that are needed in any province and any place, but vocational schools have never paid attention to them. For example, aren't tailors found in every city? Why shouldn't vocational schools open tailoring classes according to the needs of society? Vocational schools in any province should train a large number of tailors, recruiting students who have graduated from elementary school and are above a certain age and giving them considerable training. Those with clever aptitudes can make very valuable and elaborate clothes, which requires a year and a half or two years to graduate. Those with less clever aptitudes can only make ordinary clothes, which only requires half a year or a year to graduate. After graduation, the school will issue a license, or they can open their own tailoring shop or go to people's homes to work as tailors. Tailors trained in this way will definitely be much better than the many tailors who have not received education. They can not only make clothes, but they can also be called upon to bear the responsibility of promoting domestic goods (because the styles and quality of many ladies' clothes are intentionally or unintentionally influenced by tailors). For example, cooks are also needed in hotels, agencies, schools, and families. Their relationship with a group of society is more important than tailors. However, no one pays attention to such an important occupation, and it is completely undertaken by a group of people who have not received education. In major cities in China, epidemics often occur in the summer and autumn, and many people die. Some of these deaths are definitely due to cooks not understanding hygiene and food not being clean, which leads to the spread of epidemics and the loss of lives. Therefore, vocational schools in any place should open cooking classes, recruiting students who have graduated from elementary school and are above a certain age. In addition to training their cooking skills, they should also have considerable chemical knowledge and hygiene knowledge, how to arrange kitchens, how to select food, how to disinfect food, how to prevent germs, etc. Those with clever aptitudes who want to become cooks in large restaurants and hotels should receive two or three years of training. Those with ordinary aptitudes who can only handle ordinary cooking should only receive one year or one and a half years of training. After graduation, they will be issued a license, and they can run their own restaurants or be employed by others. These cooks who have received considerable education will definitely be much better than cooks who are illiterate. Not only do vocational schools train people needed by society, but the lives of a group of people will definitely be better protected.

Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools Go to Print 103

▲ To Be Published Within October

After the Ministry of Education repeatedly hired expert committee members to revise the curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools, and after the Ministry's responsible division sorted them out and the Minister approved them, the Ministry of Education yesterday delivered the entire curriculum for primary schools and kindergartens to the printer (only the Civics subject is still being sorted out and will be delivered soon). Secondary school curricula, such as Chemistry and History for junior high school, and English, History, Chemistry, Music, and Drawing for senior high school, were printed yesterday. The remaining subjects are also being sorted out and will be delivered to the printer soon. It is heard that they will be published and distributed to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities by the end of October for implementation in accordance with the newly promulgated standards.

Review Committee for Secondary School Chinese Curriculum Standards 104

(3)

The Review Committee for Secondary School Chinese Curriculum Standards convened by the Ministry of Education continued its meeting at the Ministry of Education on the 3rd, in the morning and afternoon. More than a dozen committee members attended the meeting to review the senior high school Chinese curriculum standards. (1) The original three objectives have been increased by one. The main idea of the clause is to enable students to use the national language and literature to deeply understand the inherent culture in order to achieve the goal of national rejuvenation. (2) The originally planned teaching time of four hours per week has been increased by one hour. (3) The teaching material outline has been slightly revised to (1. Intensive reading of selected texts, 2. Intensive reading of specialized books, 3. Writing, 4. Extensive reading). (4) The teaching method was discussed in part, and it was past 5 o'clock, so it was decided to continue the meeting and review it on the 4th.

Parade and Petition by Primary School Teachers in Peiping 105

▲ Unsatisfactory Reply from the Municipal Government; Establishment of a Strike Committee

Peiping, 4th: More than 400 representatives of primary school teachers in Peiping paraded and petitioned this morning, first going to the Special Commissioner's Office of the Finance Bureau, where Section Chief Rong Kun met with them on behalf of the Special Commissioner, and then going to the Municipal Government. Due to the large number of people, 11 representatives were elected, and Zhou Dawen personally received them. He promised to negotiate with the banking industry again regarding the loan, and there was no problem in reorganizing the business tax. As for future expenses, starting from September, 80% will be paid monthly. The remaining 20% cannot be demanded from the Municipal Government until the central government's funds arrive. Starting from September, 15,000 yuan will be allocated monthly to repay the accumulated debt until it is paid off. After the representatives reported to those outside, they dispersed.

Peiping, 4th: The primary school teachers' petition was unsatisfactory, and a strike committee was immediately formed. Representatives of primary school principals and teachers will go to the capital to demand funds.

Recommendation Examination for Military Instructors in High Schools and Above 106

▲ Order from the Municipal Education Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to high schools and above in the city, stating: In accordance with Ministry of Education Order No. 7842, it is approved that the General Inspectorate of Training has consulted and found that military instructors in high schools and above should have their qualifications reviewed by the Ministry, be tested, and be recommended by the Ministry for appointment. This has been done in the past. However, considering the actual situation and to avoid obstacles, in some cases, military instructors hired by the schools themselves have been reported to the Ministry for filing, and this has been temporarily approved. This should be rectified to emphasize the rule of law and benefit military training. The Ministry is now scheduled to conduct the sixth term of recruitment examinations for military instructors. All military instructors hired by the schools themselves, whether they have been reported for filing or are temporarily acting, should be recommended by the original school to the Ministry for registration and examination in accordance with the regulations, and be selected and used after being consulted and dispatched to comply with the regulations and prevent abuses. In addition to publishing the recruitment regulations in the newspaper and notifying them on the notice board of the Ministry, the corresponding recruitment regulations are enclosed, and it is hoped that they will be checked and instructed accordingly. This order (regulations omitted).

Thirty-Two Experts Co-author Student Guide 107

▲ Cai Jiemin Praises the Book as "Loving Students with Virtue and Achieving the Beauty of Students"

The book "Student Guide" is co-authored by Sun Benwen, Liu Zhanen, Wang Jun, Jiang Wenyu, Liao Maoru, Zheng Hongnian, Ouyuan Huai, Li Quanshi, Gao Jian Si, Wu Junrui, Yang Weiyu, Yu Nanqiu, Lou Tongsun, Li Yinkong, Yu Fengbin, Hu Shuyi, Zhu Shaoping, Shen Weiping, Tang Qingzeng, Wang Xishen, Zheng Tonghe, Shen Yizhen, Yu Jifan, Hu Boxiang, Jiang Xiangqing, Pan Yangguang, Zhong Zitong, Du Dingyou, Wang Yugang, Jia Foru, Liu Linsheng, and Lu Lihua, principals, professors, and academic experts from major universities and middle schools across the country. The entire book contains more than 100,000 words and is divided into two volumes. The upper volume guides male and female students of all levels in studying various subjects, and the lower volume details self-cultivation and educational advancement issues. They are all words of experience gained by the authors over decades of research. The book also includes prefaces by Cai Jiemin, President of the Academia Sinica, Cheng Shizhu, Director of Education of Fujian, and Cheng Tianfang, President of Zhejiang University. Cai praised it, saying, "Loving students with virtue and achieving the beauty of students," and it is truly a must-read book for young students. In addition to the rich content, the book is also very well bound. The price is two yuan per book, but for the sake of popularization, it is only sold for one yuan and two jiao, plus six cents for postage and seven cents for registration. It is published by Qinfen Bookstore at Shujinli Crossing, Sima Road, Shanghai, and students from various schools are now rushing to buy it.

Sports Association Warns Spectators at the Stadium 111

▲ Referees Uphold the Judgment

▲ Absolutely Do Not Arbitrarily Scold

The National Sports Association issued an important notice yesterday regarding the spectators at the stadium: The referees for various football matches organized by the association are all members of the Shanghai Chinese Sports Referees Association. Their work is purely voluntary, and they have no affiliation with any of the teams. The goal of each referee is to use their skills to judge impartially. This is the only auxiliary measure to promote sports competitions. However, spectators do not understand this and often yell and scold when they are dissatisfied, or they criticize the referee unfairly without considering their own lack of ability, treating the noble amateur sport as a performance for profit, losing the true pleasure of appreciating the skills of the game. This is an evil phenomenon in the sports field, an obstacle to the progress of sports, and even a reason for foreign countries to despise us. Therefore, we are taking the opportunity to use newspapers to make a stern admonition, hoping that all spectators will respect themselves and encourage each other in order to eliminate these bad habits invisibly. The progress of sports in our country will rely on this.

New Basketball Techniques 119

(Do not reprint) Originally written by Zhang Guoxun, Qian Yiqin, and Claire Burcky, jointly translated

Personal contact in basketball games, namely personal fouls, is one of the usual fouls. The right to declare a personal foul lies with the referees and inspectors, and others are not allowed to interfere.

Personal fouls include pulling, tripping, pushing opponents, or rushing up to grab the ball from the opponent's back, or illegal rough behavior that obstructs the opponent even without physical contact is also considered a personal foul.

There are several types of personal fouls that warrant disqualification. If both teams commit fouls against each other, it is a double foul. In some cases, the referee may also impose a penalty of two or more free throws on the fouled team depending on the severity of the foul.

If a foul occurs while the opponent is shooting, there are two possible rulings: (1) If the shot is missed, the fouled player gets two free throws. (2) If the shot goes in, the fouled player gets the points and one free throw. When two opposing players commit fouls against each other, resulting in a double foul, each gets one free throw.

Each personal foul is recorded by the recorder under the name of the player who committed the foul. If a player accumulates four fouls, they lose the right to play for the remainder of that game.

Pulling, Pushing

Sun Ke Issues Statement 120

Opinions on the League of Nations Report

▲ Points of Relative Satisfaction and Absolute Disappointment

▲ Efforts by the Government and the People Are Still Required to Recover Lost Territory

Central News Agency reports that the summary of the League of Nations Investigative Commission Report was released at 8:00 PM on the 2nd. Member of the Central Committee Sun Zhesheng especially received reporters from various newspapers in this city at his old residence on Molliere Road at 3:30 PM yesterday afternoon to comment on the contents of the report. Mr. Sun expressed disappointment with several points in the report, which are recorded below:

▲ Points of Relative Satisfaction Mr. Sun first stated that the investigation of the September 18th Incident was recorded more clearly in the report. For example, (1) in Chapter 4, the investigative commission stated that the Japanese military action on the night of September 18th could not be regarded as a legitimate means of self-defense. (2) After Japan instigated puppet organizations in the Northeast to establish a false regime, it vigorously promoted internationally that the establishment of "Manchukuo" was an independent movement of the people of the three provinces. Chapter 6 of the investigative commission report also condemned "Manchukuo" as being organized under the duress of the Japanese army and could not be recognized as an independent movement established by the people of the area. The above two points of fact were investigated and reported fairly, which is what we consider to be relatively satisfactory.

▲ Points of Absolute Disappointment Chapter 10 of the report puts forward solutions such as (1) a proposal to convene an advisory conference and not advocate the restoration of the situation before the September 18th Incident. This point needs to be studied in detail. Convening the so-called advisory conference and not advocating the restoration of the original state of the three northeastern provinces before the September 18th Incident seems to be based on violence and the established facts. We have serious doubts about not advocating the restoration of the previous state. Does this proposal refer to the state of Chinese rule before September 18th, or the military rule of Zhang Xueliang? If it refers to the former, it contradicts itself. If it refers to the latter, it should be clearly pointed out to avoid misunderstandings by the Japanese. (2) Regarding the extensive autonomy of Manchuria and the organization of an advisory conference, the result will be that the three northeastern provinces will become a nominally existent territory under Chinese control, or China's control over the three northeastern provinces will be nominal. Under the current situation, Japan has great power, and due to its close relationship, Japan will have a majority of seats in the organization of the advisory conference. In the future, the three northeastern provinces will nominally be a part of Chinese territory, but the form of governance will be international co-management, and in fact, it will be Japanese trusteeship. We express absolute disappointment with these two points.

▲ Efforts by Us Are Still Required The report is actually beneficial to Japan, while our country only gets the name. However, the Japanese government and public have unanimously expressed opposition after the report was released, which shows that Japan has long had the determination to annex the three northeastern provinces. Recalling the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, both China and Japan recognized Korea's independence, but in a few years, Japan turned against it and annexed Korea. This is a lesson from the past. Now that Japan's determination to annex the Northeast has been exposed, if we rely solely on the League of Nations, we will only get a disappointing result. At this moment, we can only hope that the government and the people of the whole country are of one mind and one heart to recover the lost land in the Northeast. According to my personal opinion, the League of Nations cannot fundamentally solve the Northeast issue. The solution depends solely on the degree of effort of our government and people, and the attitude of the international community towards the case.

▲ Views on the Boycott Movement A reporter from Xin Sheng She further inquired about the following questions, and the replies were as follows: (1) The report advocates that our country stop the economic severance of relations with Japan. Its nature is a condition for resolving the Northeast issue. In fact, the Japanese invasion of the Northeast is the cause, and the economic severance of relations is the result. If the cause is not eliminated, how can the boycott movement be eradicated? (2) The task of the investigative commission was to determine the responsibility for the Northeast incident, but the report did not dare to point it out clearly. If our country does not settle for the nominal recovery of the Northeast territory, it should prepare to resist aggression with strength, and it is especially necessary to obtain allied countries that have the same interests as ours against Japan in diplomacy.

Reactions of Various Groups to the League of Nations Report 121

The Preparatory Committee of the National People's Salvation Groups Federation sent a circular: To all newspapers, organizations, institutions, and compatriots across the country: The League of Nations bears the mission of maintaining international justice and reason in the world. Our government, on September 21st of last year due to the violent September 18th Incident in Shenyang by Japan, requested a protest to the League of Nations Administrative Council in accordance with Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant. After more than a year, the League of Nations Investigative Commission issued its investigation report. The ten chapters of conclusions clearly support the weak and suppress the strong, especially international cooperation, borrowing crutches on behalf of others, and disregarding our country. The fact of violent Japanese aggression is directly regarded as an inevitable problem, and it is also said that our people's organized economic boycott harms the harmony between countries. The so-called advisory conference, special system, and so on are all whimsical ideas that are far from the sanctity of law and the advocacy of justice, which is completely unexpected. What is the hope of our country from the League of Nations? The prestige of that League of Nations has been swept away not just today. However, before this report was released, the riddle was still there, and we still wanted to solve it ourselves. We did not know that the League of Nations was a group of powerful nations, and the Covenant was a straw dog of the world. If we do not seek our own salvation, who will seek it for us? If we do not save ourselves, who will save us? After a year of giving in with our hands, the result of being swallowed up and eaten is that we have only obtained ten chapters of written waste paper from the investigative commission, which instead raises bad advance tickets for international control of China. If we have any blood, how can we not be saddened? The enemy is deep, what can we do? This association has always had the purpose of vowing to resist to the death without yielding or fearing danger. The more we are frightened by danger, the more difficult it is to remain silent. We pray that all organizations, institutions, and compatriots from all walks of life across the country will wake up together and regard the idea of believing in the League of Nations and relying on international relations as an utterly wrong one. Let us gather all our strength and go to a new target, without hesitating any longer, without enduring any longer, in the hope that the national destiny that is about to die may be saved by chance. The telegram trembles. Please observe. The Preparatory Committee of the National People's Salvation Groups Federation bows, Branch

Huang Jinghan Comes to Shanghai; Peace Association Mediates Sichuan Conflict 128

▲ Two Lius Actively Prepare for War, Poised on the Brink

The war clouds in Sichuan Province are growing denser daily, and a conflict seems imminent. Both Lius are currently engaged in military deployments, making a large-scale war seemingly unavoidable. The inside story is quite complex. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency inquired with the Sichuan Provincial Government's Shanghai office yesterday, and the following information was deemed reliable: the two Lius are uncle and nephew, with Liu Wenhui being Liu Xiang's uncle. Initially, the relationship between the two was quite harmonious, but recent conflicts over interests have caused frequent clashes. Sichuan Province has over a hundred counties, of which Liu Wenhui's troops control seventy to eighty, more than half the province. Liu Xiang's troops, on the other hand, control only twenty to thirty counties. However, Liu Xiang's counties are all wealthy and prosperous areas, and Chongqing, the most bustling area in Sichuan, is also under Liu Xiang's jurisdiction. Therefore, his twenty to thirty counties are actually superior to Liu Wenhui's seventy to eighty counties. In the past, goods shipped to Sichuan from other provinces had to pass through the Chongqing port, where taxes were very low. Liu Wenhui had long wanted a share of the profits but had been unable to do so. Recently, Liu Wenhui ordered a large quantity of firearms and ammunition from abroad, worth over three million, and when they were transported to Sichuan, they were all detained by Liu Xiang when passing through Chongqing. Liu Wenhui was furious upon hearing this and immediately negotiated with Liu Xiang, demanding their return and passage. Liu Xiang refused. Liu Wenhui then asked for half to be returned, but this was also rejected. Thus, a grudge was formed. Although the two Lius have publicly stated that they will not engage in civil war, they are still actively engaged in military deployments. The Shanghai Peace Association sent a telegram to Sichuan urging them to cease hostilities, but received only one reply. Currently, Huang Jinghan, the political advisor of the 20th and 24th Armies of Sichuan Province, has come to Shanghai to request the Peace Association to make further effective appeals. Huang, being positioned between the two Lius, has come to Shanghai to ask for mediation from all sectors of society.

Ten American Warships Arrive in Shanghai 131

▲ Arriving from Yantai and Bohai Sea

The destroyers belonging to the U.S. Asiatic Fleet, which had been sheltering in Yantai and the Bohai Sea during the summer, were ordered to Shanghai and arrived yesterday afternoon. The first three ships to arrive were the No. 21 (USS Whipple), No. 28 (USS Parrott), and No. 226 (USS Borie), followed at 10 minutes past the hour by nine more ships: No. 212 (USS Smith Thompson), No. 228 (USS Truxtun), No. 213 (USS Preble), No. 227 (USS Bulmer), No. 219 (USS Edsall), and No. 216 (USS Edwards). An American transport ship also arrived in Shanghai at the same time. All ships sailed into the Huangpu River and temporarily berthed at Berth No. 25. Amending the Shanghai Special District Court Agreement 132

▲ The Two Ministries Agree on the Principles of Counter-Notification

▲ A Second Meeting of Commissioners Will Be Held This Week

Regarding the issue of our country preparing a note to relevant countries to amend the Shanghai First Special District Local Court agreement... The two ministries, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Justice, previously held the first meeting of commissioners to study the matter. At that time, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Justice each had a proposal on the points to be amended, and after initial discussions, it was decided to collect opinions and agree on the wording of the notes to be submitted to the various countries. According to an investigation by a New Sound News Agency reporter stationed in Beijing, the specific plan for submitting the points for amendment is currently being worked on by Yang Zhaolong, the section chief of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, who is considering and combining the opinions listed in the original proposals of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Justice to form a complete and specific plan. It has been decided to hold a second meeting of commissioners this week to discuss and supplement the opinions of this specific plan and to decide on the procedures for submitting the request for amendment to the various countries. The date for issuing the note will also be decided at this meeting, and it is expected to be issued around the end of this month.
