Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries to Adopt Domestic Coal 137

▲ The Harm of Foreign Coal Dumping Endangers the National Economy and the People's Livelihood

▲ Foreign Coal May Not Be Sold Cheaply When Domestic Coal Production Stops

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to all industries: "We hereby inform you that on the 4th of this month, we received an order from the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, She Zi No. 4253, to comply with the order. The order from the Ministry of Industry, Kuang Zi No. 4335, stated that according to the National Coal Relief Committee, the dumping of foreign coal in various ports along the Yangtze River has caused the sales of domestic coal to plummet. It has been requested that the Ministry provide relief. Zhu Yonghe, the manager of the Datong Coal Mine Company, suggested that since the signing of the Shanghai Armistice and the restoration of peace, Japanese coal has been imported in large quantities, with prices lowered to occupy the market. As a result, the sales of domestic coal have been greatly hindered. Although Shanghai has suffered less damage, sales in various ports along the Yangtze River have been greatly affected. Recently, the Hankou Water and Electricity Company is still selling coal made in Fushun, for the reason that the burning power of Fushun coal is strong. Although domestic coal has different grades, the high grade actually exceeds Fushun in power, which can be verified and is not an opinion. Many power plants in various places use domestic coal and have not heard of any cases where boilers could not be ignited. It is simply that Japanese coal is cheaper and therefore used. Factories along the Yangtze River often have this situation, which has led to the expansion of Japanese coal sales. If we do not take measures to remedy the situation, we will not be able to promote domestic goods and prevent leakage. It is requested that the chamber submit a report to the Ministry of Industry, ordering the general chambers of commerce in Jiangsu, Anhui, Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces to instruct local manufacturers to adopt domestic coal uniformly in order to clear sales channels and recover profits, resist dumping, and protect domestic products. There is no better way to do this. It was specially proposed for discussion to ask whether it is feasible and was temporarily proposed by our committee member Xie Chuang to ask the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to persuade merchants to sell and use domestic coal. A tea party was convened with various committee members to discuss this proposal. According to the investigation, the coal mines operated by foreign capital in China have all dumped by lowering prices and extending credit in order to cut off the livelihood of domestic coal and enable various sales agents to make large profits, thereby monopolizing. However, among users and coal merchants, there are many who are patriotic and do not buy foreign coal or sell foreign coal, but there are also not a few who forget righteousness for profit. Measures should be taken to stop this. According to Manager Zhu's suggestion and Committee Member Xie's proposal, they are all correct. However, to persuade factories and shipping companies to use complete domestic coal, the local chambers of commerce should publish announcements in newspapers to promote it to all sectors of society. A joint meeting of local factories and coal merchants should be convened to inform them of the harm of foreign coal dumping, which not only endangers domestic coal but also affects the national economy and the people's livelihood. If we are selfish and short-sighted, it is like drinking poison to quench thirst. When domestic coal production stops, foreign coal may not be sold cheaply, and may even raise prices and hoard. If we want to use domestic coal to recover profits and plug leaks, it will be impossible. At that time, the pain and insults will be too late. It is better to insist early, promote domestic products with group efforts, and save the situation from now on. This is the key. It is also proposed to appeal to the government to ensure that the tax rules for domestic coal mines are equal to those of foreign capital operating coal mines in China, so as to reduce the cost of domestic coal and increase production, which will provide relief. It is necessary to request the Ministry to order all chambers of commerce to implement it effectively, and also to consult the Ministry of Finance on the equality of tax rates for Chinese and foreign mine owners. The reasons are that a written report is prepared and submitted, requesting approval and implementation. In addition to consulting the Ministry of Finance on the tax rate issue, the ministry ordered the bureau to instruct the major factories and chambers of commerce to comply accordingly. This order, etc. was received and recorded and notified to you, hoping that you will check and inform your affiliates to comply accordingly.

Exhibition Notes of the China Cotton Clothing Association 138

Cheng Qing, the initiator of the China Cotton Clothing Association, held an exhibition of domestic cloth at the Qingliang Temple on Xinzha Road on October 2-3. The previous report stated that on that day, a horizontal banner was hung in the center of the venue, reading "Clothing of Great Cloth," and on both sides were couplets reading "Clothing covers the world, Weaving is a concern." The characters were large, about a foot in diameter, and were made of blue characters embroidered on white cloth. In the middle was a paper with the history of domestic cloth and suggestions for improvement. More than 800 kinds of domestic cloth were displayed in the venue. During the two days, about 3,000 people visited, and the words of those from the National Goods Company and various textile factories were the most practical and useful. Generally, rural women cannot replace their looms due to accumulated habits, so the width of the cloth is too narrow, and the yarn spun by hand is coarse, thick, and uneven. To fundamentally improve, someone must set up a factory, change to looms and factory yarn, and gather female workers, turning scattered pieces into whole units. It is best to have someone with great power lead them in an orderly and unified manner. Otherwise, looms and factory yarn must be purchased on their behalf to make the cloth. It is not easy to get them to buy it on their own. The dyeing and patterns also cannot be guided by someone without knowledge. At that time, someone gathered to discuss setting up a local cloth factory, but it is not known whether it will become a reality. Among the various cloths displayed, there were many suitable for making Western suits, as well as many items for women and children. During the two days, a total of three to four hundred bolts were sold at retail and wholesale, and more than 1,000 bolts were ordered, mostly woven cloth, which can be used to make Western suits and is especially suitable for women and children. It was unexpected that so much was sold, which also shows that the purchasing power of those who love to use domestic goods is not weak. Zhang Ji, the director of the Agricultural Education Hall, and Zhang Jinkang were responsible for collecting this cloth and explaining the improvement suggestions at the venue, which was quite painstaking. Cheng Bojia said during the two days that we are exhibiting domestic cloth, not holding a meeting, nor have we asked anyone to give a speech. I have not been on a speech stage for twenty years. I used to make a living on the speech stage in Shanxi and Zhejiang for two or three days. We want to do practical things. Meetings and speeches are frequent, but as a result, no good things are done, and people have excuses. Foreigners say that the French do things and then talk about them, the Germans talk about them and then do them, and the British do things and don't talk about them. We Chinese can be said to talk about them and not do them. I hope that all members will not use the badge of the China Cotton Clothing Association as an ornament. People say that this badge is very generous and looks good. I hope that the Cotton Clothing Association will do very generous and good-looking things as a memorial to China when it is about to be destroyed. China may not be able to avoid being destroyed. The national situation is like the six dice falling backwards, and the rivers and the sun are going down. There are too many shameless people who see profits. The poem says, "Rats have teeth, but people have no shame. If people have no shame, why wait for death?" They are really shameless things. You have also seen the foreign cloth shops on the recent roads, where people are rushing to buy foreign cloth at discounts of 40% to 50%. Goods are sold quickly, and goods are imported even faster. This is called dumping, so that everyone buys enough cheap goods, and there is no need for domestic goods. Foreigners use the psychology of people who see profits and forget righteousness to destroy the country of people who see profits and forget righteousness. It is also because we lack substitutes for foreign goods that we have to buy them. The spread of success is not strong, and no one knows that there are not a few things that can replace foreign goods, so gathering exhibitions, improving local goods, and imitating foreign goods are important things. The first exhibition is local cloth, and the second exhibition is the cloth woven by Chinese machine factories, which is similar to foreign goods and can be a substitute. However, the exhibition period has not yet been determined within the day. Although several factory comrades agree with my saying that dozens of products should be gathered for exhibition, it is not yet known whether it can become a reality, because I have no power, and I have no appeal. I wanted to invite a few people to the meeting to assist, but they did not come. Jesus said that rich people cannot enter heaven, and I don't expect them either. On that day, many people said that it is best to ask a prominent person to set an example and naturally follow the trend. Why not measure the length and width of his body, make a piece of clothing of great cloth, and ask him to wear it. Cheng said that if schools do not read the Book of Rites, people do not know the term Book of Rites or the story of Wei Wengong's clothing of great cloth. As for the prominent person, I don't know him, and I can't get close to him, let alone measure his length and width. Besides, this garment is not the yellow robe of Zhao Kuangyin's Chenqiao mutiny. Would it be put on someone's body and not taken off? Those who heard it laughed. On that day, several very short people in the venue visited the various cloths for a week and left in a hurry.

Taikoo Company's Zhoushan Steamer Sinks into the Sea 139

Taikoo Company's An Dong-class steamer, Zhoushan, struck a reef off Yantai Island on the 1st of this month, causing a breach in the bow, and the passengers were rescued. This has been reported in this newspaper. Taikoo Company is now entrusting a Japanese salvage company in Dalian to try to tow it. The Japanese rescue ship arrived in Yantai on the afternoon of the 3rd. However, because a large storm had occurred on the sea, the salvage work could not be carried out. Only a small portion of the cargo in the ship was salvaged, and the rest was still in the ship. Yesterday, the storm on the sea was even greater, the bow of the Zhoushan steamer had already broken, and the middle cabin and other places were also damaged. The hull of the ship could not support the impact of the huge waves. Yesterday, the Shanghai office received an urgent telegram from Yantai stating that the Zhoushan steamer could not be salvaged due to the deteriorating weather, and had already sunk into the sea yesterday. Most of the cargo and the crew's luggage had not been taken out, so the losses were huge. The 99 passengers who were rescued are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the company's Shuntian steamer at around 3 PM today.

Glimpses of the China Merchants Bureau's Reorganization 140

▲ Expanding Shipping Routes and Renovating Warehouses

▲ Inspecting Ships and Evaluating Crew Members

Since Li Guojie took over as the General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, he has formulated a reorganization plan and implementation steps, which were submitted to the Supervisory Office and approved by the Ministry of Transportation. The plan is being actively implemented, and considerable progress has been made. Details are as follows:

▲ Warehouse Operations. Most of the bureau's Yangtze and coastal vessels have been dilapidated. Coal has been purchased from Japan in the past. Since the Northeast Incident last year, domestic coal has been used instead, mostly from Zhongxing, Jingxing, Boshan, and the Chinese-British joint venture Kailuan. They are all purchased in bulk by the original ship, and the coal merchants supply them in installments according to the contract. The type and composition of the coal are based on a chemical test. To prevent the mixing of inferior coal, each coal ship is carefully inspected upon arrival. Most of the docks and wharves are damaged and in need of repair. The roofs of Warehouses 1 and 2 in the central warehouse have been renovated, and the doors and windows have been repaired, which were completed last month at a cost of more than 8,000 taels of silver. The repair of the bamboo fence in the Chinese warehouse cost 1,000 taels of silver. In addition, the warehouses, quays, and plum blossom piles of the North, Central, Xinhua, and Four Warehouses have been reported for bidding and will be repaired immediately. As for attracting business to the warehouses, from April to August of this year, the average monthly business was over 90,000 taels. Compared with the highest average monthly business of 80,000 taels four years ago and the lowest average monthly business of 56,000 taels, the business in May this year reached more than 130,000 taels.

▲ Expanding Shipping Operations. This year's business has been affected by (1) the decline in production due to the Yangtze River floods last year, (2) the lack of vitality after the Shanghai War, and the continued depression of people's livelihood, and (3) the requisition of ships, which prevented them from carrying as much cargo as possible. Now, the ships that were requisitioned are being gradually returned. The Yangtze River area is gradually improving. Although the Dalian and Yingkou ports on the North Sea route have been affected by the current situation, the Yantai and Tianjin ports are operating as usual. The South China route is very popular for passengers and cargo, and preparations are being made to add ships. The Xiang River shipping industry has made considerable progress. Jiangda and Kuaili have been temporarily assigned to the Xiang-Han route. Wooden sheds have been added to the Jinliyuan Wharf, street lights have been added, 14 cargo inspectors and 4 Russian police officers have been hired to maintain the order of the docks. Preparations are being made to establish an office in Qingdao. After the opening of the customs route, ships will be sent. A branch office will be re-established in Fuzhou, and Taishun will be designated as a Shanghai-Fujian liner to recover the lost business.

▲ Reorganizing Ships. All ships that arrive in Shanghai and request repairs must first be inspected for their engineering. Important projects must be surveyed and estimated first, and an estimate form must be prepared. The factories submit bids to undertake the project, aiming for low prices and solid workmanship. The electrical equipment of each ship is inspected, the cargo hold volume of each ship is measured, and the heating surface area of the boiler of each ship is measured for auditing purposes. As for the regulations on the service of crew members and the regulations on repairing ships, they are being planned. Senior crew members are also being assessed for promotion, and the resumes of junior crew members are being registered to facilitate promotion. The diligence of those on duty is inspected to serve as a standard for attendance. The procedures for applying for coal are streamlined, and the reasons for application are thoroughly reviewed.

Silk Factory Labor Strike Yesterday 141

▲ Two Factories Resumed Work Yesterday

After the female workers of various silk factories in the concession area went on strike again the day before yesterday, two factories, Yuyuan and Chuxin, resumed work yesterday. The silk factories in the Hongkou area remained closed. The details are as follows:

▲ Two Factories Resumed Work. Since the female workers of various factories in the Three Districts (concession area) went on strike again on the afternoon of the day before yesterday (the 4th), the labor and management sides have not negotiated. Yesterday morning, the factories still blew their whistles as usual, urging the female workers to go to work. At the same time, the police sent a large number of detectives to protect the factories. As a result, 70% of the female workers from the Yuyuan and Chuxin silk factories on Guoqing Road in the Chinese area went to work, and the police station sent police to maintain order. The female workers from the five factories of Xiangfeng, Jingwei, Xiangyuan, and Chang on Gansu Road and Alaersituo Road did not go to work, so the factories immediately stopped the silk machines.

▲ Hongkou Situation. The silk factories in the Hongkou area remained closed yesterday, and work remained suspended. Most of the striking female workers were waiting quietly at home, so there were no disputes. The labor union investigated the recent silk prices and prepared a table, which was sent to the Social Affairs Bureau for verification.

▲ Yichang Moves to Wuxi. The Yichang Silk Factory has ceased production.

After settling the workers' wages the day before yesterday, the arrears of wages before September were paid out at 1 PM yesterday. The female workers in each department of the factory also went to the factory on time to collect their wages. It is reported that the factory has now rented the Tai factory outside Wuxi's two gates to continue operating. The factory's employees will be taken to the new factory in Wuxi. Yesterday, a group of employees left Shanghai. However, a group of employees were introduced by the landlord and are planned to be dismissed immediately. The employees have requested that severance pay for two months be issued and have requested the union to negotiate with the factory.

▲ Union Reports. The Silk Industry Union of the Third District reported to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday: "Regarding the renewed strike of the workers of Xiangfeng Silk Factory, etc., we request that the matter be investigated and handled. The female workers of various silk factories in our district went on strike automatically because they could not bear the exploitation of the factory. Later, after the union sent personnel to persuade them, they resumed work on the 26th of last month, waiting quietly for a solution. However, the workers of Xiangfeng Silk Factory, etc., have waited for many days and have not seen a solution. They suddenly went on strike again yesterday afternoon. The union has no way to deal with it. We hereby send this letter to report and request that you quickly approve it. It is truly in the public interest.

▲ Municipal Government Instructions. The Municipal Government is paying close attention to the silk factory strike. Fearing that the dispute would be prolonged and affect local security, after receiving the report from the Social Affairs Bureau, the government specially instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to quickly resolve the issue.

▲ Negotiation Method. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Municipal Party Department, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau negotiated to resolve the silk factory strike dispute. At 2 PM yesterday, representatives of the Silk Factory Trade Association, Shen Huachen and Zhang Peishen, were summoned for talks. The head of the mediation section, Wang Xianqing, received them. According to the demands made by the union, the capitalists were persuaded, and the following was decided: (1) The workers should resume work first, and the labor and management sides should jointly be responsible for persuading the workers. (2) The government will be responsible for investigating and dealing with those who cause trouble.

▲ Union Letter to Association Sets Deadline for Reply

All workers in the Shanghai letterpress printing industry went on strike last year due to the issue of working hours. Fortunately, it was resolved through government mediation. Now, due to the impact of the war, the employers are refusing to comply with the labor-management conditions, and the workers are angry. The Letterpress Printing Industry Union reported the situation and argued according to reason. Yesterday, in addition to sending a letter to the employers' trade association, the union also reported to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Department, ordering the employers to earnestly fulfill their obligations. The original text is as follows: "Regarding the letterpress printing industry's employers failing to fulfill the conditions, privately making agreements and ordering workers to obey, oppressing workers, destroying the labor movement, and dismissing workers in large numbers, we request that you severely stop this and implement the terms. The Zhonghe Printing House forced workers to change to contract work and ordered workers to pay rent. The Meili Printing House discounted wages, paying only 70%, and dismissed 23 workers in batches, privately formulating regulations to force them to obey and instructing workers to leave the union. Other factories, such as Shengsheng Printing House, have also dismissed workers in large numbers and forced the contract work system. The future of the labor movement has been destroyed, and the workers' livelihoods have been cut off. The union, in consideration of the imminent destruction of the country and the disturbance of the Red bandits, has decided not to provoke incidents. At a time when the Chinese people are uniting to resist foreign insults, the employers are disregarding humanity and public opinion, oppressing workers and destroying the labor movement, which is unfortunate. In addition to sending a separate letter to the employers' trade association to earnestly fulfill their obligations and setting a deadline for a reply, we hereby report the situation of oppression to your Ministry Bureau Association, and respectfully request that you approve and order the employers to earnestly comply in order to avoid disputes, relieve the workers' difficulties, and facilitate the progress of the industry. It is truly in the public interest." Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Party Department, Social Affairs Bureau, and General Labor Union.

法公董局徴方單地税 143

▲Negotiation by the Municipal Government Based on the Situation

The Jiang Yu Ji Construction Factory on Route Tenant de la Tour in the French Concession of this city was subjected to ultra vires taxation and unreasonable interference by the French Municipal Council. They retained lawyer Jiang Zongpan and requested assistance from the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession. The association considered this matter related to national sovereignty and sent a letter to the municipal government to lodge a protest. The municipal government yesterday lodged a strong protest with French Consul General Meyrier. The original letter is transcribed below:

To Whom It May Concern:

According to a letter from the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Shanghai Public Concession, based on a letter from lawyer Jiang Zongpan, Jiang Changlin of the Jiang Yu Ji Construction Factory stated that in the area of Route Tenant de la Tour No. 222 in the French Concession in 1920, he leased a piece of land, identified as a "fangdan" (property deed registered with the Chinese authorities) property, from Chen Genfa and others, measuring three mu, on which several bungalows were built for temporary use as storage and a workshop. For many years, everything was peaceful. Unexpectedly, in August of this year, the French Municipal Council suddenly ordered the payment of 358 taels and 9 mace of land tax, arguing that the land was "fangdan" property and had no obligation to pay the tax. After a reasoned reply, on the morning of September 20th, the Council sent people to forcibly seal off the entire frontage of the property with lead wire, preventing entry and exit, and detaining workers inside, disregarding the freedom of residence acquired by the people under the law.

It is noted that the nature of a concession and a leased territory is absolutely different. The establishment of a concession only designates an area in which foreigners are allowed to lease land to establish residences. Therefore, except for land leased through deeds with foreign nationals in the concession and its road areas, "fangdan" properties are, according to law and custom, exempt from land tax. The reason is that "fangdan" properties are owned by Chinese and still pay national tax and surcharges, and are not leased to foreigners. Therefore, the Council has no right to collect land tax. Even if payment is required, it should be collected directly from the landowners, not from the tenants. Now, the Council is violating the agreement, breaking customs, illegally levying taxes, and without going through legal procedures or filing a lawsuit in court, it is using coercive means to seal off the warehouse, in effect forcing people to do what they are not obligated to do. This is a small matter of infringing on individual legal rights, but a major matter of undermining the agreement and harming our national sovereignty. Moreover, the lives of more than a dozen workers detained inside are at risk, which is absolutely inhumane.

It is noted that the Public Works Department of the Public Concession previously attempted to collect land tax, but after legal contention by the Chinese Taxpayers Association, it was immediately canceled. The present case is the same and must be fought for to safeguard sovereignty. It is requested that the situation be communicated to the Shanghai Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association for assistance.

The situation is as stated above. It is requested that you investigate and handle the matter. According to the documents, the "fangdan" land in the concession area, according to the words and spirit of international conventions, based on legal principles, the municipal authorities of the concession have absolutely no right to collect land tax. The Public Concession has had similar incidents, which were exempted after the association fought for them according to law. The Public Concession authorities are particularly able to be convinced by law in this case, which is admirable. Moreover, the French Concession authorities, in addition to the blockade, detained workers, which is even more unacceptable to humanity. According to the above, it is requested that your government promptly negotiate to protect sovereignty, which is a matter of public concern.

According to this, it is requested that the situation be investigated and clarified, and that the actions be promptly rescinded. This is addressed to Mr. Meyrier, French Consul General in Shanghai.

中華醫學會大會第五日記 148

The Fifth Day of the Chinese Medical Association Conference

The Chinese Medical Association continued its business meeting yesterday morning. At 10:35 AM, Mr. Okey, a London statistics expert, gave a presentation on the importance of statistics in medicine, stating that the use of medical science, regardless of basic or clinical materials, is limited if statistical methods are not used for precise analysis. Members attending the meeting then participated in discussions, and the results were summarized as follows:

(1) Statistics is not valued because its format is boring and tasteless.

(2) Most hospital physicians in various places have heavy duties, and it is difficult to supply systematic materials.

(3) Disease terminology is diverse and complex, making it difficult for statisticians to start.

In order to correct the above shortcomings, physicians in various places should use a uniform format to record daily clinical materials precisely, compile them, and submit them to statistical experts. Mr. Okey will make an overall analysis, compile them and send them to the members, and disclose them in the Chinese Medical Journal.

The discussion ended at 12:30 PM. After lunch, group meetings were held for five groups: obstetrics and gynecology, dermatology, radiology, pathology, and physiology.

At 4:00 PM in the afternoon, members went to Renji Hospital on Shandong Road for tea, and others visited the Public Works Department's Health Department. Renji Hospital also performed internal medicine and surgery demonstrations in the research room on the fifth floor.

At 9:00 PM in the evening, there was a tea party at the private residence of Sir Candali at No. 6 West Great Road. Male and female guests were at the peak of fashion, with melodious music, fragrant clothes and beautiful hairpins, and everyone dispersed in joy.

上海虎疫時期已過 149

The Shanghai Cholera Epidemic Period Has Passed

The Director of the Public Works Department's Health Department reported to the Board of Directors that the cholera cases in the Public Concession and surrounding areas have now moved away from being epidemic.

It is noted that around May 30 of this year, the cholera cases in Shanghai reached an epidemic level, and on June 6, the Public Concession and the roads outside the boundary also reached an epidemic level. According to the standards for calculating whether an infectious disease has reached an epidemic level, if an average of three patients are reported each day within a week, the area is considered epidemic. According to statistics for the past week, there were a total of three cases of cholera in the Public Concession, with no deaths.

閘北自來水重訂水價 151

Readjusting Water Prices in Zhabei

According to the Central News Agency, the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company's previous cancellation of bundled water and widespread installation of water meters caused disputes among landlords, companies, and users. The municipal government stipulated four compromise measures in August 1929. The implementation period was originally until the end of 1931. As the expiration date was approaching, the company believed that most of the existing bundled water users were poor, and the cost of installing water meters would be higher than bundled water. Fearing that landlords would use this reason to raise rents to tenants, for the benefit of the poor, the company's board of directors resolved to stipulate four special price measures and reported them to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for review and transfer to the municipal government. Later, the war broke out and the matter was suspended. It is now reported that the measures have been approved by the municipal government and will be implemented. The details are as follows:

(1) For existing bundled water users whose rent is below 12 yuan, the water price can be calculated at a special price when water meters are installed.

(2) The implementation period of the above-mentioned special price is set at two years, ending on December 31, 1933.

(3) The special price, regardless of the amount of water used, is set at 1.5 jiao (cents) per 1,000 gallons, or 7 fen (cents) per cubic meter.

(4) If the landlord holds shares in the company, the water fee can still be calculated at 90% of the special price according to the shareholder's water usage preferential method.

漁業各團體代表大會 153

Fisheries Organizations Representatives Conference

▲Resolved to Oppose Government's Collection of Fisheries Tax

▲Yu Qiaqing Telegraphed Request to Cancel the Proposal

Upon hearing that the government intends to implement a fisheries tax, the fishery organizations in this city convened a representatives conference of fishery merchants yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the Ningbo Guild Hall. Representatives including Yu Houtai of the Seafood Fishery Association, Wu Tingsheng of the Salted Fish Association, Ge Liquan of the Taizhou Fishery Merchants, Bao Bingheng of the Maofeng Fishery Company, Mao Jusheng of the China Fishery Company, Zhai Jiujun of the Fresh Fish Guild, Yu Zhenqing of the Shanghai Fishery Association, and Dai Taohang of the Fishery Merchants Customs Brokerage, totaling more than 60 people, attended the conference. Yu Houtai was elected chairman. After reporting on the government's intention to implement the fisheries tax, the following resolutions were passed:

(1) Organize a Fishery Tax Exemption Maintenance Committee. Each organization will send one to five representatives to participate in the organization. Organizations that have not yet attended the conference are requested to participate successively.

(2) The internal expenses of the committee will be borne by two types of sponsorships: Type A, 800 yuan; Type B, 500 yuan.

At the same time, Yu Qiaqing, a leader in the fishery industry, telegraphed the government requesting the cancellation of the fisheries tax. The original text is as follows:

(1) Nanjing, respectfully presented to Chairman Lin of the National Government, Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan, and Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry: Upon hearing the news of the revival of the fisheries tax, fishery merchants and fishermen are running around in distress and telling each other. It is noted that the exemption of the fisheries tax was implemented by order on March 28, 1921. A sudden reversal seems inappropriate to show good faith to the people. Currently, taxing material objects is purely a transit tax. It is not appropriate to reopen this evil precedent after the abolition of likin (internal transit tax). In recent years, the fishery industry has declined and is on the verge of collapse. Millions of fishermen are on the brink of bankruptcy. Protection is not even possible, let alone exploitation. What is felt to be dangerous must be reported. It is earnestly requested that a decisive decision be made to immediately cancel the original proposal. It would be a great blessing for the fishermen and the party and the country. Yu Qiaqing kowtows.

(2) Jiujiang, Mount Lu, respectfully presented to Chairman Jiang Jieshi: Upon hearing that the ministry is discussing reimposing the fisheries tax, fishery merchants and fishermen are running around in distress and telling each other. Last year, on March 28, a new decree was issued clearly exempting the fisheries tax. A sudden reversal now, how can we show good faith to the people? Moreover, the fishery industry has declined greatly, and the fishermen are already in a dangerous situation of bankruptcy. To drain the pond to catch fish is not a good idea. It is hoped that you will uphold the exemption that was previously in effect and maintain it in the future. Please immediately telegraph the Executive Yuan and the ministry to cancel the original proposal. It would be a great blessing for the fishery industry and the party and the country. Yu Qiaqing kowtows.

A Public Banquet for Tang Huisun from All Walks of Life

At 6:00 PM the night before last, people from all walks of life held a public banquet at the Atlantic Restaurant on Sima Road for Mr. Tang Huisun, the former director of the Agricultural Affairs Office of the three provinces of Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, who had recently returned from an inspection tour in the West. Those who attended included Tang's companions, entomology expert Cai Banghua, forestry expert Lin Weifang, Chen Zhenpeng, a technical expert from the Ministry of Interior, Wu Juenong, a technical official from the Ministry of Industry, Pan Xixiang, the director of the Wuxi Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Factory, Wu Hengru, the chief of the second section of the Social Affairs Bureau, Song An, the director of affairs of Lehua Girls' Middle School, Guo Ping of the Quanchong Guild, Wang Chengjun, a consultant to the Qingdao Municipal Government, Shi Shukang, a representative of the Agricultural College of Zhejiang University, Sheng Siding, a representative of Zhengfeng Girls' Middle School, Tang Hanlin, a lawyer and older brother of Tang, and Mrs. Brainerman, a newly hired German professor, totaling more than 30 people.

Chairman Zhou Dingchang gave a banquet speech, stating that Mr. Tang had profound research on agricultural administration. This time, Zhejiang Province sent him to Europe and the West to inspect agricultural administration, and he traveled to more than 20 countries. After returning to China, he must have a detailed and good plan for revitalizing China's current declining and exhausted agricultural administration.

Recent photo of Tang Huisun

Mr. Cai Banghua and Mr. Lin Weifang have studied in Western Europe and have many writings. They are expected to make great contributions to the two sciences of entomology and forestry. Mrs. Brainerman is a famous German scholar who has traveled a long distance to China to teach. We are even more deeply impressed.

Tang then gave a speech stating that our country has a vast territory and abundant resources. There are many agricultural fields where mines have not been opened or excavated. As long as the people do their best and fulfill their responsibilities, working hard, the imperialists, although ambitious, will eventually bow down and admire our country one day. I hope that all sectors of society will join hands and come together, which will not only be a blessing for our 400 million compatriots, but also a blessing for the weak nations of the East.

Mr. Cai Banghua and Mr. Lin Weifang then gave speeches and reported on their experiences and feelings during their trip to Europe, with many poignant words (details omitted). Finally, Mr. Chen Zhenpeng encouraged his comrades who had returned to China to continue to work hard with the attitude of a world-class academic researcher in order to obtain considerable benefits.

The banquet ended at around 9:00 PM. Also, it is reported that Mr. Tang Huisun will immediately pack his bags and go to Zhejiang University to teach.

A Vendetta Case Occurs in Western Shanghai

▲Approximately 30 Years Old

▲More Than 20 Stab Wounds

The Sixth District Second Sub-Station of the Xujiahui Town Municipal Public Security Bureau in Western Shanghai reported to the station at around 4:00 PM yesterday that a villager had reported finding an unidentified male corpse murdered in the cotton field north of the Zhujia Tomb Mountain behind Zhujia Stone Bridge on Xuhong Road in the west of the town.

Director Liu immediately sent police officer Xue Jinxian and others to investigate. The corpse, approximately 30 years old, was lying in the field with its head facing south and its feet facing north. There were more than 20 knife wounds on the head, face, neck, chest, etc. The wounds were approximately one inch wide. The eyeballs were protruding, the flesh was blurred, and the scene was tragic. The upper body was wearing a blue striped foreign cloth turn-down collar shirt, blue old cloth trousers, white cotton socks, and pointed-toe shoes. The head was flat. He looked like a worker. It is assumed that he was murdered. There were many maggots on the head. It is likely that he had been dead for two or three days. A piece of white paper written in pencil was left by the roadside, with the words "Please, comrades, act as agents for the Jiangbei person, the one from Zhenjiang who comes the most, the one who abandons the most people, the black-hearted fried-hearted traitor" and a Shanghai Inland Water Company's 21st year October No. 1694 Xiaoqiaotou vegetable market stall No. 92 water price two jiao receipt, with a Tan Shunchang stamp on it. It was immediately taken to the station for investigation. Because time was short, the corpse was guarded by the local security chief Zhang Qintuan, and it will be examined this morning.

Local News Two

Mr. Qian Qizhong, Clerk of the Second Branch of the Commercial Court, Appeals 157

▲ Sentenced to One Year in Prison Due to the Ye Shantao Case

▲ Appeals the Original Verdict

Ye Shantao, a shareholder and director of the Gongfa Company, was previously sued by Dong Longxing and others, creditors of the Riyue Bank, for forgery. When the second instance was being conducted at the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, a man surnamed Wu suddenly visited Ye, claiming to be dispatched by Qian Qizhong, the clerk assigned by Judge Zhao Zhengtao who was hearing the case. He asked for a bribe of two thousand yuan, promising to give him an advantage in the case, otherwise, the debate would be reopened, and it would certainly be disadvantageous. Ye ignored him. Later, the case was pronounced on June 27, sentencing Ye to three months in prison, suspended for one year. After receiving the verdict, Ye believed that the presiding judge and clerk were adding charges because their demand for money was not met. In addition to declaring his disapproval of the verdict, he filed an appeal with the Supreme Court. Furthermore, his attorney, Lu Shaozong, officially wrote to the Ministry of Judicial Administration of the National Government, requesting a thorough investigation. Subsequently, Minister Luo instructed Chief Prosecutor Wang of the Second Branch of the High Court to order Chief Prosecutor Zu Ze of the First Special District Local Court to conduct a strict investigation. Chief Prosecutor Wang summoned Qian Qizhong, clerk of the Second Branch of the High Court, to court for several interrogations. At the same time, he personally went to the Second Branch of the High Court to inquire with Judge Zhao Zhengtao of the Criminal Division, who was handling the Ye case, about Qian's inquiries into the case details at that time. After the investigation was concluded, it was determined that Qian Qizhong was suspected of attempted fraud and dereliction of duty. Therefore, based on the Criminal Law, he was prosecuted to the Criminal Court of the same level. After Judge Wu Zhen's trial, the defendant was sentenced to one year in prison and allowed to be detained in the court's detention center during the appeal period. However, Qian was unconvinced after receiving the verdict. Because the first instance treated this case as a primary case, he could only appeal to the local court of the original court. The grounds for his appeal were detailed in both factual and legal points. However, the prosecutor of the initial prosecution also disagreed with some parts of the first instance verdict and had also filed an appeal. Yesterday afternoon, Qian Hongye, Chief Judge of the Criminal Court of the First Special District, along with Judges Shen Bingying, Ge Sidong, and Prosecutor Guo Wei, specially opened a criminal court to summon witness Ye Shantao and examine Qian's case. Qian Qizhong presented his appeal, claiming that he was assigned to Judge Zhao Zhengtao when he was a clerk in the Second Branch of the High Court. The initial verdict of his guilt was based on Judge Zhao's testimony. However, Judge Zhao was the first defendant, and it was difficult to accept his words as the basis for convicting a co-defendant. Moreover, his statements before and after were often inconsistent. He had only gone to Zhao's place twice. Once was in early June, when Zhao returned to Shanghai from Suzhou and gave him melon seeds, so he went to his residence to thank him. The other time was after the verdict of the Ye case, Zhao had also come to his residence four times. This was simply a social interaction and there was no solicitation. As for the so-called Mr. Wu, he first said he was sent by the clerk when he went to Ye's house, and then claimed to be a representative of the judge. Who exactly was Wu? He did not want to, so his words were even less credible. The debate in the Ye case concluded on June 21, and he was transferred to the Document Section on the same day. Chief Judge Qian then read to Qian the confession of Judge Zhao during the investigation, in which Zhao said that Qian had gone to his house twice to inquire about how the Ye case would be judged. He also asked that if there was no solicitation, why did Zhao make this confession? Qian replied that only Judge Zhao himself knew the reason. However, according to Ye Shantao's confession, he learned on June 24 that the case would be reopened for debate. According to Judge Zhao, he only told him about the reopening of the debate on the 25th. These two statements were inconsistent. He and Ye did not know each other. Subsequently, witness Ye Shantao testified that a man surnamed Wu visited him around 3 or 4 pm on June 24, claiming to be sent by Clerk Qian, asking him to embellish the case. He initially asked for five or six thousand yuan, then reduced it to two thousand yuan, otherwise, the case would not be pronounced on the 27th and would have to be reopened for debate. He also said that if he did not believe him, he could bring the clerk with him the next day. However, only Wu came alone the next day, so he never fell for his scam. He also knew that his case was justified and would not lose the lawsuit. His lawyer, Lu Shaozong, also advised him not to be deceived. Later, the case sentenced him to three months in prison. He was extremely angry and believed that he was convicted because the extortion failed. He discussed it with Lawyer Lu, and Lu wrote to the Ministry of Justice to investigate, stating that he and Clerk Qian did not know each other. Chief Judge Qian pointed out that Ye's confession was somewhat different from what he stated in his letter to the Ministry of Justice, so he repeatedly questioned him. After the defending lawyer for Qian Qizhong presented his arguments, Chief Judge Qian ordered that the case files of Ye Shantao be reviewed and a date be set for further interrogation.

Wu Huaichun Accused of Rape of Two Daughters 158

▲ Young Daughter Dies from Rape

▲ Older Daughter Enticed and Abandoned

▲ Mother Files a Private Prosecution

▲ Asks for Conviction and Compensation for Losses

Wu Huaichun, residing at No. 24, Jiwu Fang, Ximen Road, Yinyu Company, and Fan Guilin, residing at No. 2, Zengrong Li, west of Beichujia Bridge in the French Concession, were recently sued by Shi Chen, a woman from Changshu, and her 19-year-old daughter Jinghua, who entrusted lawyers He Yijun and Yu Peng to file a private prosecution with the Second Court of the Special District for crimes of raping a young daughter, causing her death, and raping and enticing her older sister, etc. The indictment stated that they were accused of raping a young daughter, resulting in death, and raping and enticing her sister, maliciously abandoning her. It requested the court to detain and interrogate them, severely punish them according to the law, and also included a civil lawsuit. Shi Chen had two daughters, the elder being Jinghua and the younger being Lingyu. Jinghua was born on the 19th day of the first lunar month of the third year of the Republic of China, and Lingyu was born on the 25th day of the ninth lunar month of the seventh year of the Republic of China. They both studied poetry and books in their youth. In November of the 19th year, Lingyu came to Shanghai with relatives and resided at the home of the second defendant, Fan Guilin, at Chujia Bridge. Lingyu had a beautiful appearance. After the first defendant met her, he enticed her in various ways. Lingyu was only thirteen years old and her awareness was weak, so she lost her virginity to the first defendant. In the fourth lunar month of this year, she was enticed by him to live together at No. 14, Chengqing Li, Bair Road. Lingyu, at this age, was not fully developed, and she was devastated and fell ill and died on the 15th day of the fifth lunar month (i.e., June 18th) at the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road. When she was seriously ill, Jinghua, mindful of sisterly affection, rushed to Shanghai from her hometown day and night to take care of her, not closing her eyes for seven or eight days. On the night of the 24th day of the fourth lunar month (i.e., May 29th), Jinghua, unable to overcome her fatigue, fell asleep on the bed for the first time. Who knew that the first defendant suddenly had evil thoughts and developed beastly desires? Taking advantage of Jinghua's sleep, he secretly untied her trousers and forcibly raped her. When the two sexes made contact, Jinghua woke up and resisted, but it was impossible. The first defendant threatened that alarming the patient would hasten her death. Jinghua had no choice but to let him do as he pleased. Afterwards, Jinghua was filled with shame and pain and wished she could die. The first defendant repeatedly used sweet words to deceive her and threatened her at the same time, insisting that Jinghua live with him and promising to cancel Jinghua's engagement with her fiancé. Jinghua was inexperienced and was moved by him, so she followed him and lived together in the Wuling Apartment on Bair Road. Who knew that the first defendant would become tired of her after a long time and his attitude would change drastically after a few months, abandoning Jinghua. Jinghua had no choice but to return to her hometown, harboring grievances and weeping all day long. Shi Chen felt that something was wrong. After questioning, she learned that the first defendant was so unlawful and no better than a beast. Shi and Jinghua came to Shanghai on the 21st of this month to negotiate with him. The first defendant relied on his wealth and power and ignored them. He especially maliciously abandoned Jinghua. The first defendant first raped a young daughter, causing her death. Then he raped and enticed Jinghua, and finally abandoned her, insulting women to the extreme. His actions clearly violated Article 240, Paragraph 2 and Paragraph 4 of the Criminal Law, the crime of raping a young daughter causing death, the crime of taking advantage of the opportunity to rape in Article 241 of the same law, the crime of enticing a young daughter in Article 257 of the same law, and the crime of abandonment in Article 290 of the Criminal Law. The second defendant is suspected of assisting the first defendant in raping the young daughter and should also be dealt with according to the law. Although the first defendant owns property worth over one million yuan in Shanghai, the facts of his crime are very serious. The lightest sentence for the crime of raping a young daughter is more than seven years, and the lightest sentence for the crime of rape causing death is life imprisonment. It is especially difficult to avoid escape. Therefore, in accordance with Article 42 and Article 43 of the Criminal Procedure Law and Article 4 of the Agreement of the French Concession Court, a private prosecution is filed, requesting your court to approve the direct detention of the defendant without summons for interrogation and to punish him according to the law, and to order him to compensate for the losses of 100,000 yuan and to pay Jinghua's living expenses of 100,000 yuan, etc. It is said that the indictment has been submitted to the court and the trial should be held soon.

Commander Zhang Ying Extorted by Discharged Soldiers 160

▲ Discharged Soldiers Claimed Commander Deducted Pay

▲ Feared He Would Flee, So They Sought Him Out

Zhang Ying, who resided at No. 3 Qingfu Li, Jing'an Temple Road, and was formerly the commander of the 59th Division of the National Revolutionary Army, was suddenly visited by four discharged soldiers from the division, Li Shuliang, Jiang Qingmei, Wang Gancheng, and Tang Yun, around 12:00 on the 22nd of last month. They broke into Zhang's house, searching for Commander Zhang and his wife, and threatening them with handguns. When they saw that Mr. and Mrs. Zhang were not there, they left in disappointment. Witness Cui Xianting also testified that the defendants came on the 22nd of last month with handguns, claiming to be looking for Commander Zhang's wife and son, saying that they were there to avenge the killing of the division's member Zheng by Commander Zhang. When they saw that the wife was not there, they went upstairs to search and left. The next day, they received a threatening letter and reported it to the police to send detectives to arrest them. Defendant Wang Gancheng confessed that Commander Zheng of the 59th Division was shot and killed by Commander Zhang last month for asking Commander Zhang to pay the arrears of salary. Not only were they indignant at the time, but all the soldiers of the division unanimously expressed their indignation. However, they were not subordinate to Commander Zheng's department. The reason for this was that Commander Zhang had deducted military pay, and the soldiers reported it to the Military Commission, which ordered an investigation. Fearing that he would escape upon hearing the news, they came to Shanghai to find him. Furthermore, Commander Zhang was proficient in martial arts and very strong. Fearing that they could not defeat him, they borrowed two handguns from a friend, preparing to hand him over to the police after finding the commander. He said that the threatening letter was written by Tang Yun, who was on the run, and he did not know about it. Tang had told him that he had reached an agreement with Commander Zhang, who agreed to borrow 2,000 yuan to return to his hometown. He could go to Tiantong'an tomorrow to meet the representative of Commander Zhang carrying a leather suitcase, and invite him to Hongkou Park. He went there and was arrested. When questioned, Li and Jiang's confessions were the same as Wang's. After the two lawyers debated, Judge Ge Sidong reviewed the confession and concluded the debate of the case, setting the verdict for next Tuesday. The defendants were still taken back to the police station for detention.

Private Red Pill Factory Cracked Down on Zilaihuo Street 167

▲ Two Red Pill Kings Arrested

▲ Each Person Paid a Large Sum to Bail Out

Lu Changfa and Qian Zubei (also known as Qian Guodong, nicknamed Xiaoshandong), the red pill kings, specialized in making red pills from morphine and other toxic powdered drugs and selling them throughout the interior. Countless people have been harmed. The French police, led by Chief Detective Sa Tsai'er, Detective Li Liansheng, and Detective Bao Fang Zhaolin, etc., discovered that Xiaoshandong's factory was located at No. 46, Ruifu Li, Zilaihuo Street. They went quietly the night before, confiscated dozens of packs of red pills and silver dollars, etc., and arrested five people, including Bao Xiaojingli Shi Yinbao, clerks Chen Degen, Yuan Kexia, Cao Nanshan, and Yu Shengkang, who confessed the whereabouts of Xiaoshandong. They immediately rushed to arrest Zubei and brought him to the police station. However, Lu Changfa escaped without a trace. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the case, and stated that the defendants violated Article 6 of the Prohibition of Opium Law. However, some procedures were not yet prepared in this case, and the accomplices had not yet been arrested. He requested an extension of the hearing. When questioned, Qian Zubei confessed that he worked as a waiter in a certain hotel and did not dare to make red pills privately. He gave evasive answers to the remaining questions. Shi Yinbao confessed to privately selling red pills, but the red pills were purchased from Xiaoshandong and Lu Changfa. The official asked why he bought red pills from both of them. He replied that some people specialize in smoking Xiaoshandong's goods, and some people specialize in smoking Lu Changfa's goods, so it is true that he bought goods from both places to sell. Chen Degen confessed that he had been working at Shi Yinbao's place for a short time. Yuan Kexia and the other three confessed that they went to Ruifu Li to visit friends and did not dare to help make red pills. They gave evasive answers. The defendants also retained lawyers Jiang Yiping and Zhu Dianqing to defend them. Judge Xiong ordered Qian Zubei to pay a bail of 8,000 yuan, Shi Yinbao to pay a bail of 3,000 yuan, and the other four to pay a bail of 1,000 yuan each to be released, pending a rescheduled hearing.

French Language Tutoring Evening Class at the Sino-French Institute of Technology 168

The Sino-French National Institute of Technology is an educational undertaking jointly run by the Chinese and French governments. All kinds of science are taught directly in French, cultivating talent. In order to facilitate those who are interested in learning French, a tutoring evening class is attached. The first class will tentatively enroll 30 students, from 6:00 pm to 7:00 pm, with one hour of class per day. There is no tuition fee. Classes will start on October 17. Registration will be from 6:00 pm to 7:00 pm on the 12th, 13th, and 14th. The outline is as follows: Article 1 (Purpose) is specifically to provide an opportunity for those who are interested in studying French. Article 2 (Tuition) is purely voluntary and no tuition fees are charged. However, students must provide their own books and supplies. Article 3 (Duration of Study) is tentatively set at two years. Article 4 (Age and Qualifications) There is no age limit for admission, but those who are already studying at other schools will not be accepted, in order to avoid concerns about neglecting one for the other. Article 5 (Guarantee) Before admission, a reliable Shanghai merchant must fill out a guarantee to ensure that the applicant is of clear background and good character. Article 6 (Deposit) In order to prevent students from abandoning their studies midway, students must fill out a volunteer form and pay a deposit of 5 yuan in national currency when entering the school. The full amount will be refunded at the end of the semester, but if there are more than one-fourth of the lectures missed, the deposit will not be refunded. Article 7 (Supplementary Provisions) This outline may be amended at any time if there are any omissions. Article 8 This outline was formulated on October 1, 1932.

Joint Meeting of the National Medical Association's Executive and Supervisory Committees 174

The National Medical Association held its second session of the second Executive and Supervisory Committee meeting yesterday at the Jinlong West Tea House on Nanjing Road, Shanghai. Attendees included Executive Committee members Xu Naili, Yu Yunxiu, Wang Qizhang, Cai Yumen, Jiang Zhenxun, Zhu Qiluo, Pang Jingzhou, and Supervisory Committee members Wang Wanbai, Mao Xian, and Hong Borong. Discussions: Item 1: The resolution passed by the general assembly regarding proposals numbered Chinese characters 9, 15, 16, 17, 22, 32, 37, 45, 46, and 49 concerning the establishment of a pharmaceutical factory. Decision: A special committee consisting of Yu Yunxiu, Cheng Mugu, Wang Wanbai, Hua Yunsun, Wang Qizhang, and Xie Yunshou was previously formed to discuss the matter, but it was deemed extremely difficult. Therefore, the association can only promote domestic production in principle and support and promote various domestically produced pharmaceuticals. The method:

Members can be notified to report the results of already tested domestically produced products to the association. Item 2: The resolution passed by the general assembly regarding proposal numbered Chinese characters 31, which advises national doctors to organize a society interested in pathological anatomy. Decision: Yu Yunxiu and others were appointed to draft a proposal. Once the draft is completed, colleagues will be solicited for their opinions. Item 3: Medical education issues. Decision: The Medical Education Special Committee will proceed as appropriate. Item 4: Pang Jingzhou proposed and Wang Wanbai seconded that, due to concerns that the composition of foreign drugs is unclear in the interior, leading to confusion during use, the association, with its abundant talent, may as well conduct preliminary reviews to promote their use. Decision: The principle was approved, and Pang Jingzhou was asked to plan the implementation. Item 5: Due to the original address being insufficient for use, the association will relocate to 41 Chihang Road, Aiveni Road, Shanghai, the office of the Chinese Medical Association. Decision: Approved. The relocation will be carried out after the 16th of this month. Item 6: The general assembly passed resolutions on the following pending cases: (1) Chinese characters 6, 19; (2) 12, 21; (3) 25; (4) 29; (5) 33, 41. Decision: The secretariat will organize and handle them. The meeting adjourned at 4 PM.

Free Talk

Two or One Branches of Talk

Prohibition of Private High Schools 189

— Zhan Lu

One of the proposals passed by the meeting of education bureau directors is to prohibit private middle schools from adding high school divisions. This is a severe measure to eliminate private middle schools. It has been resolutely and bravely proposed and passed, and the day of implementation is probably not far off. However, what will happen after implementation?

Recently, it has been extremely difficult for junior high school graduates to enter provincial high schools. The number of places is only dozens, but the number of applicants is often seven or eight hundred, or even close to a thousand. This is the situation in Jiangsu. It is said that the Guangzhou area is even more crowded, with thousands of junior high school students competing for these dozens of high school places. The qualification for high school is simply unattainable, similar to passing the imperial examination and becoming a successful candidate in the old times. Every time the list of successful candidates is announced, it causes great sorrow among many who failed, teaching them to taste the flavor of taking the county exam during the imperial examination era. At this moment, their only savior is the provincial high school. Although it is full and regrettably lacking, private high schools still have surplus places to fill. At least half of these failed junior high school graduates rely on being accommodated in private high schools to avoid being out of school.

If private high schools are prohibited, and public high schools cannot be specially expanded and added according to the proportion of junior high school graduates, then every time junior high schools graduate, the number of junior high school graduates who cannot study will suddenly double. In the past, failed county examination candidates could rely on their ability to recite Confucius and Mencius to make a living as tutors. What is the level of junior high school graduates now? They cannot write essays and cannot carry water. Cutting off their path to advancement, what do you want them to do sitting at home all day?

Esteemed directors of education bureaus, did you have a hard time at the meeting? Are you all well? May I ask, in passing this magnificent proposal, are you encouraging reading or advocating for people to be out of school?

China's Soldiers 190

— Qi Wo

In his article "Observing Turbulent China," Japanese scholar Tsurumi Yusuke said that a certain politician, a former prime minister of China, once told him: "Today's China is like medieval Europe. For example, if you ask a soldier, 'What kind of soldier are you?' he will immediately answer, 'I am General Zhang's soldier,' 'I am General Feng's soldier,' 'I am General Tang's soldier.' Three hundred years ago, when soldiers in the streets of Paris were arguing, if you asked them what kind of soldiers they were, they would answer, 'I am a soldier of the Duke of Neschli,' or 'I am a soldier of the Duke of Olen.' But what about now? Everyone says they are soldiers of the French Republic. "China is the same. At present, soldiers all say they are Zhang's soldiers, Tang's soldiers, Feng's soldiers. When that day comes, perhaps they will answer that they are soldiers of the Republic of China. Until that day arrives, the current state will continue!"

This comparison between modern China and medieval Europe not only makes these foreign observers feel deeply interested, but even those of us in the country who are concerned about politics feel that this statement truly reveals China's current hidden problem! Honestly speaking, although China's cities are immersed in the color of 20th-century capitalism, and China's politics are adorned with many golden signs, the soldiers in China are still nothing more than warriors from the feudal era, and the military leaders in China are nothing more than feudal lords. Zhang cannot mobilize Feng's soldiers, just as Feng cannot mobilize Zhang's soldiers. Feng's soldiers belong to Feng, and Zhang's soldiers belong to Zhang. No one else can control them. What is the difference between this and the Five Hegemons and Seven Heroes of the Warring States period?

With such a feudal-style army, China will never be unified. No matter how much politics is on the right track and the economy is prosperous, if the military still has factionalism in their hearts, it will all be in vain! I believe that the day when Chinese soldiers understand that they are soldiers of the Republic of China will be the time when China is truly unified, and the time when the crisis of civil war in China is forever eliminated.

Five-Flavored People 191

— Sun Zongwen

Sour, Bitter, Sweet, Spicy, Salty

Yesterday's dinner at home was not very satisfactory, why? Because: the vinegar fish was too sour, the smoked chicken was too bitter, the pineapple honey soup was too sweet, the mustard chicken was too spicy, and the salted duck was too salty. Therefore, none of these dishes suited everyone's taste. Everyone said in unison: "This chef is not very good!"

Because of yesterday's meal, I thought of how we humans are not so different. A person's mental attitude is different due to the inherent instincts and the environment of life, thus creating different personalities, just like the five flavors in a dish, but not so obvious.

(1) Sour people are mostly forced by the environment and become humble after repeated setbacks. Although this type of person's strength lies in humility, there will be no arrogance. However, if he is asked to handle a matter alone, he will inevitably delay the opportunity due to a lack of decisiveness! (2) Bitter people are depressed all day long, and it is not easy to see a smile on their faces. Their words are also full of bitterness. This type of person is mostly those who are frustrated, unemployed, or heartbroken. It is not easy to hope for their development!

(3) Sweet people are always optimistic and good at understanding people's psychology, taking people's intentions as their own. His strength lies in making people not dislike him, but he has no independent opinions. If things go wrong, there is no solution!

(4) Spicy people are bold and daring. No matter what happens, he can make judgments and have solutions. He does not care about feelings, does what he thinks of, and speaks frankly and deeply. But he is just stubborn and does not listen to other people's advice, and he will make things worse!

(5) Salty people, saying that this type of person is stupid, but not stupid. Saying that he is smart, but not smart. If there is no clear person to guide him well, the future is the most dangerous!

Therefore, it is important for people to be moderate. People who contain only one flavor, although they have strengths, cannot hide their weaknesses and must be cultivated. Otherwise, it will be like a dish with only one flavor, and no one will want to learn from it!

Powerful Tragedy 192

— Ming Yi

Guaranteed to Make You Cry

The success of film art lies entirely in its power to move people. Figures like Clara Bow, who use "flesh" to attract attention, are not considered moving, so they are only praised by a group of erotic maniacs.

Lillian Gish's mournfulness and Ann Harding's poignancy do have a very deep power to move people. Films like "Revenge" and "Orchid of the Empty Valley" leave an indelible mark in the depths of the audience's hearts.

This can also be said to be a somewhat comforting thing! Among all the Chinese actresses, there is not a flashy star like Clara Bow, but there is a tragic star who combines the strengths of Lillian Gish and Ann Harding. Who is she? She is Chen Yumei, who advocates frugality to save the country.

She had already made a good impression on the audience in the silent film era. Since starring in the sound films "Aunt Yunlan" and "One Night of Luxury," the audience's faith in her has been further guaranteed. Her lily-like clear and beautiful appearance, lake-like quiet temperament, and seagull-like ethereal attitude are fully expressed on the screen, making people feel as if they are in a poetic and picturesque realm, looking up at the bright moon and listening to the flowing spring.

Her most recent film, "The Lost Trail in Orchid Valley," is a grand tragedy depicting the oppression under feudal society! I dare to believe that if this film were starred by another actor, at most, they would move the tragic story to the screen without missing a single detail, which would be considered fulfilling their duty. But she really does more than that! When the film had an unofficial test screening at the New Light Theater the day before yesterday, several fragile-hearted women were crying aloud when they saw the last few scenes. When the lights were turned on, everyone in the audience had red eyes. No matter what tragedy a reporter watches, they only admire its artistic quality and will never cry. The reason is, "Crying while listening to storytelling is worrying about the ancients." It's too silly, but that day my eyes were a little moist, because the several close-up shots in the hospital gave me too deep a stimulus!

It is said that "The Lost Trail in Orchid Valley" will be released to the public soon. Undoubtedly! Chen Yumei's art will give us a deeper understanding!

Postal Journey into Guanzhong (5) 193

— Seeking Happiness

Today, a wife of a high-ranking officer named Gao came to my house. My aunt specially introduced me to her, which held me back from coming to meet you earlier. However, that is a small matter. I also heard them talking about how Officer Gao's superior, Commander Li, wanted to find a young female student to be his fifth concubine. This Mrs. Gao was planning to recommend me. If the matter is successful, not only will she get a sum of money, but she also promised to promote my uncle to be a county magistrate or a tax bureau director. There are so many benefits, and what is sacrificed is only my irrelevant, poor child. How could my aunt and uncle not be happy to comply? I was very anxious when I heard this. As soon as the clock struck seven, I made the excuse of going out to attend a night tutoring class, grabbed my bag and rushed here, wanting to discuss with you a good way to deal with and rescue me." After saying this, she began to sob softly.

"This is outrageous!" After a moment of silence and distress, he suddenly let go of her hands and clenched his fist in the air, gesturing and saying, "What right do they have to sell you to someone else as the fifth concubine through a business transaction? Won't you defend your right to freedom of marriage and not recognize this illegal marriage contract and resist them officially?"

"It's easy for you to say," she said with a bitter smile. "Of course, I don't recognize their selling me by such despicable and devious means. If it weren't for this, I wouldn't have come to tell and discuss with you. But you have to think more for me. I am a weak woman. No matter how hard I resist them, I can only argue with them in words on the surface and cannot prevent them from plotting and scheming at any time. There will be many dangers in the future. I can't stay in this pit of fire anymore! I need to get away from them as soon as possible and find my own way out!"

She became more and more excited as she spoke, and her voice became higher and more passionate. But when she said this, she suddenly changed to a more intimate tone and seductive attitude, slowly approaching him, as if she were delicate and powerless, wanting to lean on him. He, because he had never experienced such great tenderness, was a little shy. Also, due to the large number of tourists in the garden, he was afraid of being laughed at, so he stepped back little by little. But she could not restrain herself and followed him closely. Finally, she grabbed his left arm, placed half of her face diagonally on his shoulder, and softly said to a slightly secluded grassy slope behind the pavilion, "Brother Boqin! Don't you understand my heart? In the past two months, I met you at your cousin's English tutoring night school, and we became very good friends. My passionate heart is almost completely dedicated to you! The only difference is that my entire body has not yet been formally entrusted to you.

If something like this happens, I will be taken by someone else if I am not careful. At this critical moment, I can no longer hesitate so much and ruin my life. I can only frankly express myself to you, asking you to accept my pure love as a virgin, rescue me from this sinful and dangerous realm, let me be protected and cherished by you for the rest of my life, and jointly create a beautiful and happy new life!"

Commercial News

Financial Market in Turmoil 194

▲ Fluctuations Reaching Eight Taels: Yesterday's Gold Market was Quite Chaotic, Characterized by Unpredictable Fluctuations and a Lack of Certainty. Throughout the Day, Prices Hovered Around 730 Taels, with a Fluctuation Range of Approximately Eight Taels. Ultimately, Compared to the Previous Day, Prices Rose by Three Taels. The Supply and Demand in the Market were Complex, and Investor Sentiment was Unstable. The Market Opened with a Rise, but Due to the Minimal Increase in American Silver, it was Unaffected. However, the Loose Foreign Exchange Market and Speculative Enthusiasm from Various Parties were Unsustainable, Leading to a Sharp Decline. Subsequently, Bills of Exchange Stabilized, and Although the Official Rate Extended Slightly, the Underlying Rate Remained Firm. Furthermore, Sellers Re-entered the Market, and Foreign Exchange Short Positions were Covered. Additionally, the Central Bank Resumed Spot Trading, Causing Market Prices to Rise Again. At Noon, Prices Reached the 30 Taels Mark. The Afternoon Market Initially Fell but then Strengthened, with Strong Demand. After Some Fluctuations, Prices Exceeded the Morning's High, Reaching 31.4 Taels. Ultimately, Prices Fell Slightly by Just Over One Tael. The Central Bank Purchased a Total of 525 Gold Bars in Spot Transactions at Prices ranging from 27.5 Taels to 30.05 Taels, Sold Through Da De Cheng, Qian Chang Xiang, and Other Dealers. Below is a Detailed Account of the Day's Events.

▲ Unstable Morning Market: The Market Opened at 11:00 AM, with an Increase of 2.8 Qian, Reaching 730.09 Taels. Although American Silver Rose by 1/8, Private Telegrams Only Indicated an Increase of 1/16. Large Bars Remained Unchanged, and the Forward Silver Market Rose Slightly, so There was No Impact. Subsequently, Prices Declined, but Only by a Few Qian. Heng Xing Made Purchases, While Zhi Feng and Yong Ze Sold. Later, the Foreign Exchange Market Loosened. HSBC Offered October British Gold at 1/9/1/25 and Hua Bi Offered American Dollars at 30.5, Followed by November at 6/25. Additionally, Yuan Kang Xiang, Heng Xing, Heng Yu, Yi Feng Yong, Zhao Feng Chang, Fu Tai Ting, Fu Yu, Yuan Xing Yong, Shun Mao, and Others Engaged in Heavy Selling, Causing Prices to Plummet by Over Seven Taels. The Recovery was Only About One Tael. At 9:24 AM, Prices Settled at 23.5 Taels. Heng Xing Suddenly Made Purchases Again, Immediately Adding Over Two Taels to Reach 25.8 Taels. In an Instant, Prices Retreating to 4.2 Qian. At 9:30 AM, HSBC Posted Rates, Extending British Gold by 2/5 and American Dollars by 3.75, but Gold Prices Did Not Fall, Remaining at 25.45 Taels, Because Short Positions had Already Been Taken. Subsequently, HSBC and Others Absorbed January American Dollars at 93.75, While Hua Bank Absorbed at 8.75, and the Current Month at 56.25. Furthermore, Tian Feng, Yong Da De Cheng, Fu Yu, Heng Yu, Yuan Heng, Rui Xing, Zhi Feng, Yong and Others Rushed to Buy. Heng Xing Continued to Buy. The Central Bank Sold October American Dollars at 56.25, Hedging with November Bars, Causing Prices to Rise Above 27 Taels. However, From 9:30 AM to 10:30 AM, there was a Fluctuation of Over One Tael. Afterwards, Fu Yu, Da Xing Yong, Rui Xing, and Others Bought Again, and the Central Bank Absorbed 420 Spot Contracts, Sold by Qian Chang Xiang and Da De Cheng, to Offset Bar Positions. Hua Bi Also Absorbed January American Dollars at 8.75, and Half a Yuan for the Current Month, with Both Purchases and Sales Permitted, Further Boosting the Gold Market. At 11:30 AM, Prices Reached 30.06 Taels. Heng Xing Suddenly Sold, Causing Prices to Drop to 29.3 Taels. Rui Xing, Wan Xing, and Yu He Entered the Market to Buy, Again Raising Prices to 30.02 Taels. Unexpectedly, Heng Xing Sold Limit Order Bars Again. By Noon, Prices Closed at 29.5 Taels. After the Afternoon, Due to Bank Account Deposits and Withdrawals, Prices Fluctuated Around 30 Taels for Ten Minutes. The Unpredictability of the Market Was Baffling.

Flour: Initially Weak, then Attractive 208

Yesterday's flour market opened with a flat and then attractive outlook. Because foreign wheat prices briefly declined by 1-2 jiao, the market initially seemed weak. However, Tianjin merchants became active. Active purchases occurred for the current month (reportedly, purchases for troop transport require an additional 3 fen). Forward contracts were also purchased. Furthermore, major flour mills did not offer sales. Small mills such as Xiang Xinhuafeng did try to sell, but due to solid sales, investor sentiment rose. Prices rose by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day's closing. By the afternoon, near and far-term prices were hovering in place. Because overall, there were few positive signs as there are rumors of an Australian harvest, with private telegrams quoting 3.9 taels. Canadian wheat was quoted at just 3.77-8 taels. As domestic rice prices decline, it seemed impossible to achieve a natural average. Flour mills will have no advantages in the future. Ultimately, the current to December prices rose 1.35 fen, January rose 1.5 fen, February and March rose 1 fen.

Wheat Market Changes 209

Yesterday's wheat futures market hovered and showed a slight upward trend. Although foreign wheat prices declined slightly by 1-2 jiao, there were no large sellers on the market. Many firms had contracted for foreign wheat last year and had plenty of delivery orders. This year, although foreign wheat prices are lower, most of those contracting are factories, and few traders are asking. Therefore, although the environment is not good, it is considered dangerous to completely sell all positions. Once trading stabilized, the market outlook improved.
