Surprisingly Few Actual Transactions After Tin Price Increase 214

In the spot tin market, the previous increase in Singapore and London drove up prices in the local market as well. Initially, end-users and merchants took advantage of the opportunity to monopolize the market, resulting in considerable actual transactions. However, due to tight credit conditions, the upward trend inevitably stalled, leading to a significant decrease in outgoing orders. As for market prices, due to the shortage of incoming goods and dwindling inventories, prices have been maintained at current levels without falling. Dutch tin is priced at 100 taels per dan, Fukien tin at 103 taels, Hengdi tin at 96.5 taels, Jianghua tin at 98 taels, sheet tin at 98.25 taels, Tongde tin at 96.5 taels, and hook light tin at 51.2 taels, while solder is at 50 taels.

Observations on Falling Oil and Asphalt Prices 215

The asphalt market should have been active after the Mid-Autumn Festival, but it has been sluggish this year. It has been weak since autumn, and it was initially thought to be a temporary situation, expecting a turnaround when autumn sales began. However, the market has continued to decline, deteriorating further. The situation is increasingly unmanageable, and panic is widespread. Hankou first lowered prices, followed by Hangzhou. Although local dealers do not have large inventories, they are affected by Hankou and Hangzhou. Moreover, Hangzhou can sell throughout the interior, further blocking sales channels. In Hankou, factory oil has fallen to 14 taels, and Chongjing oil has also dropped to 15.68 taels, although inventories are said to be low. However, sales cannot be maintained without price cuts. Hangzhou is experiencing even more chaotic and disorderly price cuts, with no fixed procedures. Prices have lost their standards. Although Neiping oil is quoted at 25 yuan, sales vary. Some customs oil with slight moisture is sold for less than 20 yuan, making a market price impossible. According to Hangzhou dealers, they have been losing ground whenever prices rise or fall in recent years. Those selling outside are even more disorganized, losing their direction and steps. This is also a market vicissitude. Local dealer prices are supposed to be fixed, but in this market, fixed prices are merely nominal. However, inventories are not high everywhere, and new supplies are still far off. Those who are calm are not worried, while those eager to sell are in a panic. Therefore, although the market is declining, attitudes vary.

Supplement to the Shanghai Shenbao

Comments

From Improving Society to Promoting Children's Education 216

— Cheng Xun

If the statement "Today's children are the masters of tomorrow" is considered true, I urge parents and elders in society to pay more strict attention to children's education.

Children's minds are pure, and their spirits are lively. How should we nurture their keen thinking and instill rich intelligence? Let them build the nation and benefit society in the future. If we follow old habits and fail to provide good education, leading to thirteen- or fourteen-year-olds writing lengthy love letters and bizarre dramas of leaving home to seek immortality in the mountains, I cannot help but cry for the future of the nation!

Parents should first discipline themselves. Constant mahjong and card games at home can tempt children to gamble. Numerous servants can foster children's arrogance and laziness. Quick tempers and harsh words can cultivate children's stubbornness and snobbery. If parents do not eliminate bad habits themselves, discussing children's education is futile. Instead, bad influences may be deeply injected into children. I see many parasites in society and think of these irresponsible parents.

So-called children's education does not necessarily involve rigid and tedious lectures. At any time, in any place, and with any object, there are good opportunities to provide children with good education. I would like to write about a few of the most needed things.

1. Cultivation of frugality, hardship tolerance, and a fair attitude.

2. Instilling basic knowledge and scientific understanding.

3. Planting the spirit of integrity, cooperation, and love.

4. Practicing physical training and military exercises.

We are certainly not comparable to foreign societies in terms of economic wealth and the perfection of children's educational facilities. Therefore, children are indeed unfortunate not to enjoy profound and comprehensive education. However, at a minimum, we should promote the above four aspects of education to foster children's thinking and prepare them to be masters of the future.

Finally, I hope that parents will not think that their children beating the neighbor's children means they have a brave spirit, or that constantly reading novels about flying swordsmen and immortals means their children are studious. And do not think that feeding children well and keeping them warm and plump is the end of your responsibility! You still need to consciously educate these children.

Arts and Literature

Autumn Swallow 217

— Ran Nong

Desolate alleyway, early morning bridge,

Soul silent before, swallow brings news of flowers,

Most comforting is the memory of Zhu Fang mistaken by birds,

Events murmur, emotions separate, illuminating spring,

What's the matter? Cold, freezing, obscure words,

Sound returns, love, couples, warm sun, taking.

Autumn, no, love, couples, lingering twilight, remember return.

Science

Prevention of Fruit Tree Diseases 218

— Hai Sha

This journal's science column has always been about industry and physical chemistry, and has not detailed issues such as agronomy. I will first describe an article on "Prevention of Fruit Tree Diseases" to contribute to this column, which I think readers will be happy to hear about.

Most Chinese people cultivate fruit trees by relying on favorable weather and geographical conditions, letting them grow naturally. They rarely have adequate research into pests and other diseases. Often, when fruit trees are harmed, they only know to cut off the damaged bark or branches, or pick off the affected fruit, but do not know to use medicine for prevention before diseases occur. Therefore, I have excerpted several points for horticulturalists to know.

(1) Pear and Apple Rot: This disease initially appears as reddish-brown, then slowly develops blisters. The skin becomes sticky and soft, often occurring on the branches of apples and pears. It is most likely to occur in unsettled weather. There is a milky white liquid inside, which gradually dries up, causing the fruit and branches to rot.

Treatment: Apply "Bordeaux mixture" (Bordeaux mixture recipe attached below) in early spring before the disease occurs to prevent it. If there is disease on the branches, they must be cut off and burned to prevent transmission.

(2) Pear Black Spot and Red Star Disease: This disease occurs on branches and young shoots, and also on the fruit. When it occurs on the fruit, the fruit is not symmetrical, and the diseased area will hinder growth. When it occurs on the leaves, it is black or sooty, with black spots in a circular shape that easily fall off when touched, causing the branches and leaves to slowly wither and fall off. Red star disease has the same symptoms, but the color is red, and the spots are smaller.

Treatment: Apply "Bordeaux mixture" during flowering and fruiting. However, do not apply it when a tree is in full bloom. Only pick off and burn the diseased leaves and fruit.

(3) Peach Leaf Curl: This disease occurs on peach leaves and young shoots, causing the leaves to become thick and curled. The inner layer of curled leaves turns grayish-white. Mild cases cause only yellowing and leaf drop, while severe cases will stop fruit growth.

Treatment: Spray "Bordeaux mixture" once when peach blossoms are about to open, once when they are in full bloom, and once after the petals fall off to avoid the disease.

Attached: Bordeaux Mixture Manufacturing Method: Ingredients: 1 catty of quicklime, 1 catty of copper sulfate (i.e., gallstone), 60 catties of clean water.

Tools: Two small wooden buckets (do not use copper or iron), one large wooden bucket, one chaff sieve (i.e., a bamboo sieve for sifting chaff).

Method: Fill the two small buckets with 4 or 5 catties of water. Place copper sulfate in one bucket and lime in the other. Stir the bucket with copper sulfate with a small stick until it is evenly mixed with the water, then pour in 25 catties of clean water. Then place the bamboo sieve on the large wooden bucket and simultaneously take the liquid from the two small buckets (stir the bucket with lime into a milky white color and mix with 25 catties of clear water) and pour it into the large bucket from the bamboo sieve. Discard the coarse material stopped by the sieve. At this time, stir the liquid in the large bucket with a stick, then immerse blue test paper (sold in pharmacies) in the liquid in the large bucket. If the paper does not change color, the liquid is successful. If it turns red, then add a little lime water to make the medicinal properties uniform, so as not to harm the fruit trees due to excessive strength.

Social Improvement Discussion Group

My Views on Reforming Entertainment 219

— Tong Sheng

Indeed, everyone should have what is called entertainment as a human need. It is something we cannot lack and is an essential condition of life. Besides the necessities of food, clothing, and shelter, it is more important than anything else. Therefore, you see that regardless of whether it is in China or abroad, ancient or modern, regardless of farmers, merchants, laborers, or students, from the supreme to the poor worker, the wise or the foolish, everyone has one or more kinds of entertainment.

The basic condition of entertainment is to make us happy. It is a way to compensate the spirit and soothe the mind after mental and physical labor. It can strengthen our bodies, invigorate our spirits, and promote our careers. It is closely related to us and should not be despised or lacked.

The meaning and effect of entertainment have been briefly stated above, but looking at the current habits in Chinese society, we are too disappointed. It has not only lost the essence of entertainment but has also turned into a boring pastime. The entertainment that the public currently recognizes has already taken a deformed path, such as watching horse racing, dog racing, gambling, flower associations, etc. The most prevalent is mahjong.

There are many such bad social phenomena, and I cannot list them all for discussion. Now I will take mahjong as a representative. Looking at Shanghai as a basis, I can say decisively that about six or seven out of ten people play mahjong, and most of their lives are spent on it. Mahjong certainly has its fun, and we can appreciate it. However, they have become money worshippers in this fun, and they even regard it as a daily career, playing eight rounds and then another eight rounds, night after night, wanting to win some money. As a result, they get the following:

(1) Exhaustion of spirit

(2) Wasting time

(3) Wasting money

(4) Neglecting relatives and friends

(5) Cultivating laziness

(6) Promoting cunning

(7) Gambling away money and losing morale

The unreasonable entertainment in today's society has all these points, but they enjoy it and do not know how to abstain. They do not get the taste of entertainment but suffer much boredom, and even ruin their families and lives. This self-inflicted suffering is truly a pitiful thing.

In my humble opinion, the following work should be done on entertainment:

(A) Negative aspects

1. The government should strictly prohibit unreasonable entertainment.

2. Everyone should reflect on themselves and ask themselves "Why" after the fact, as Mr. Hu Shih said.

3. The government should investigate and deal with places that sell unnecessary entertainment venues and tools.

(B) Positive aspects

1. The government must vigorously promote public entertainment venues such as parks, sports fields, cinemas, and playgrounds.

2. The government should conduct "conscious entertainment" propaganda.

3. Encourage models of true entertainment.

4. The government should act as a model for the public.

5. Prepare conscious entertainment tools at home, such as organs, phonographs, chess, sports equipment, and play equipment.

6. The head of the family should act as a model and guide their children to prevent them from going astray.

The entertainment problem in today's society really needs to be reformed, but no one notices it. My purpose in raising this issue is to hope that everyone will rise up and carry out reforms, and at least make everyone pay attention to this issue. That would be the greatest blessing of this article.

A Corner of Society

Be Careful with Coins! 220

— Xiao Heng

"Wang Ma, take this lead eight-cent coin and pay the vegetable seller, and tell him to give you back eight copper coins. Be careful! It doesn't matter! These country bumpkins don't know how to tell the difference between foreign coins. Didn't I pay him the same way last time? That's right! I remember he even gave me back more than three hundred cash! I got it for free!" Mrs. Li hadn't finished her proud words when Wang Ma had already taken the lead coin and walked out the door.

"Hey! Vegetable seller, here are two eight-cent coins. Give me back eight copper coins." Wang Ma followed her madam's orders and gave the lead coin to the vegetable vendor, but at the same time, with an attitude of pity and unfortunate sympathy, she softly said, "Be careful with coins."

"What a joke! Your family is a regular customer. How could you trick us?" After receiving the lead coin, the vendor, because he heard Wang Ma's advice, didn't even bother to look at the lead coin and quickly hid it. Quickly and hastily, he gave Wang Ma back eight copper coins. This was his extreme expression of belief and sincerity in gratitude to them! "Pig, real pig, hee!"

After receiving the eight copper coins, Wang Ma unnaturally laughed coldly, laughing and scolding the vendor according to her madam's criticism. Of course, it was not to despise him or be mean to him, but it really contained two meanings: pitying his stupidity and being annoyed that he could not accept her advice. However, since the country vendor, who had always been called a "pig" by customers, heard her say, he thought she was bantering with him.

Although the vendor didn't recognize the lead coin, the moneylender proved its identity to him two hours later. Needless to say, could the moneylender take such a lead coin? As a result, the vendor had to exchange another real coin for it. However, the family's living expenses for one day ended here. The vendor's wife also had a fight with her husband, forcing him to exchange it back from someone the next day, and saying, "Last time, using a lead eight-cent coin made the whole family hungry for a day. If we keep being blind like this, there will be a day when the whole family starves to death!" After a quarrel, she was so angry that she lay in bed and refused to get up!

Country people still have some pig-like temper. Having suffered this loss, how dare he ask someone to exchange it? Early the next morning, selling at the door of the Li's house, Mrs. Li and Wang Ma both came out and stopped him, bought vegetables and paid. The vendor sighed to Wang Ma:

"After all, your family is so proper. Yesterday, this old grandma even said to me, 'Be careful with coins.' Who knew that after I went back yesterday, I found two lead foreign coins, which made me pay the moneylender and I had no money for food. Poor my woman, she had a quarrel with me and went hungry, and she is still sick today!"

Mrs. Li smiled slightly at Wang Ma after hearing this, indicating her victory. Wang Ma didn't say a word, and only after the vendor turned his back did she sigh softly and weakly spit out two words:

"Pig."

School Scene

Make-up Exam 221

— Man Qian

S School can be said to be very famous in Shanghai! Their make-up exam system for students who fail is like this: Students who fail two subjects in an academic year are allowed to take a make-up exam. If they fail more than two subjects, they are not allowed to take a make-up exam and are announced to be repeating a year! Of course, if they can pass the make-up exam, they can be promoted. Otherwise, they will have to study for another year.

The school authorities are also very considerate of the students. Whenever a student happens to fail three subjects, they always add the score of the better subject to 60 points to give him a chance to take a make-up exam. Therefore, several years of history tell us that students who repeat a grade must have failed three or more subjects.

The make-up exams are usually held in the three days before the official start of classes after the start of the school year. As usual, each student has to pay one and a half yuan in make-up exam fees for each subject. The results of the make-up exams are usually PASS. Because the invigilation is not strict during the make-up exam, only a registrar who is always regarded as a plaything by the students stands there. Therefore, it is possible to cheat, such as having someone take the exam for you, sending missiles from the window sills, copying from cheating notes, passing exam papers, etc., all of which are common tricks. If you are really unlucky and your score is still not good, then you can go to the teacher who teaches the course to beg and plead before the results are announced. The stories of two students I know about the make-up exams this semester are good examples:

Student C, he had to take make-up exams for two subjects this semester, but he was too clear about the make-up exams, so he was very careless and didn't go to school until three days after the make-up exam had been held. According to the rules, those who do not ask for leave and do not take the make-up exam must repeat a year and will not be allowed to take the make-up exam again! However, F was an exception, but he was promoted unconditionally without being tested! Ah! The reason is that he is the nephew of the director of academic affairs.

F was also too careless. He always thought that the make-up exam was not a problem for promotion, so he just played all day during the summer vacation and threw the books aside without even looking at them. However, this time he was just unlucky. When he was taking the make-up exam for XX subject, he happened to meet the principal who came to inspect, so all his tricks and abilities could not be used. As a result, he had to bite the bullet and submit a blank paper! Of course, such a score is really too much. Even C himself knows his fault! Finally, for the sake of promotion, he had no choice but to lower his body and go to the teacher who taught the XX subject to beg! What teacher would be so picky as to make things difficult for others? Because of one subject, you will not be able to be promoted! So he was happy to do a favor, handed the blank paper back to F, and told him to rewrite it in the dormitory and submit it to the Academic Affairs Office. In this way, the difficult situation was solved!

Therefore, S School has no so-called make-up exam. As long as you are qualified to take the make-up exam, you will always PASS, but you have to pay one and a half yuan for each make-up exam!

No Way Out

Grief 222

— Hui

The pain and sorrow of unemployment for half a year filled his entire soul: all his grand ambitions and extravagant desires were exhausted! Every day, he just lived in "hope" and "expectation"! Waiting, waiting, hoping for tomorrow today: when tomorrow comes, he looks forward to the coming of next week. However, the gift that next week brings to him is still "pain" and "sorrow"?

Relatives and friends gradually expressed their helplessness. After his earnest requests, they finally put on a terrible look of disgust, saying as if reprimanding and caring at the same time: "It's not fun to be unemployed in Shanghai. Let us raise travel expenses for you to go back to your hometown."

Shanghai is indeed hopeless, but isn't going back to his hometown the same as having no chance of survival? His only hope is to start looking for job advertisements in newspapers.

"Ah, a ray of dawn!" When he discovered that a school wanted to hire a hardworking and tireless teacher, he was overjoyed, as if the god of victory had thrown himself into his arms! So he respectfully wrote an application letter with sincerity and eagerness, and went to the post office to register it and send it. On the third day, as he wished, he received a reply letter, the general meaning of which was: they had decided to hire him to take on the senior grade level, with a monthly salary of twenty yuan, calculated for four months per semester, without food and accommodation, forty hours of teaching per week, and requiring a cash deposit of sixty yuan. If he was willing to accept, he could bring the money within three days to negotiate. Although the treatment was harsh to the extreme, he thought it was better than waiting to die idle. Moreover, he had always had the character of "not being afraid of being busy, but worrying about being idle," so the burden of work was not a problem for him; the problem was the source of the deposit, which made him deeply troubled and anxious. He could not help but resent and curse the cruelty, cruelty, and hypocrisy of mankind. Would a primary school teacher abscond? He had no choice but to go and discuss it with relatives and friends who advised him to return to his hometown. After three whole days of running around, appealing, begging, and crying, he managed to raise less than twenty yuan. He was also afraid of delaying the appointment date, so he had no choice but to take the money to the school to discuss it! He asked them to accept the money first and deduct it from his salary later. However, the reply he received was:

"Sorry, we cannot accommodate you. This is the decision of the school board."

With glistening tears in his eyes, he stepped out of the school gate; he thought, "Am I destined to be a vagrant! Or is society giving me a special gift?"

Deceived

A Love Listening Gramophone 223

— Shi Ben

The real, hypocritical, and morbid world is simply full of thorns and darkness. Slippery careers and deceptive dealings are like bamboo shoots after rain, more and more every day. The methods used are becoming more and more wonderful. If you are careless, you can fall into its trap. However, all kinds of scams cannot escape using "bait" to lure you into the game. Therefore, if you want not to be deceived, unless you adhere to the principle of "do not be greedy for small gains," then, even if there is "bait" in front of you, you will not be caught. If you do not do this and like to be greedy for small profits, you can form the fact of being deceived everywhere!

Mr. Shi next door is also a friend who is greedy for small gains. Whenever he discovers something cheap, he always rushes to be the first to take action, trying to get there first. However, the facts have told him several times that trying to get cheap always results in being taken advantage of instead. However, although he has encountered "trying to steal a chicken but losing the rice," he still has not realized it and is still often in the maze of "trying to get cheap," so this time there is another mess:

One day, he read a certain newspaper and found in the advertising column a cheap advertisement that said, "Give you a lovely small gramophone." Below was also attached a "Here is a coupon for two dollars. Please give us a Love Listening brand small gramophone, two records, and a box of steel needles. To the Advertising Department of Shanghai XX Foreign Firm." He was so happy that he jumped up after reading it, thinking that he could get a gramophone for the cost of only two dollars. It was really an unprecedentedly great bargain. He couldn't miss this wonderful and rare opportunity, and he could conclude that it was the foreigners (referring to foreign firms) who wanted to sell the "Love Listening" brand, so there was such a special great sacrifice. In the future, when their brand is sold, don't say they will give it away, I'm afraid you won't even be able to buy it. Thinking of this, he couldn't help but feel elated. The psychology of greed for small gains was immediately fully revealed. He immediately cut off the coupon, took two dollars, and ran to the post office to remit money to Shanghai. On the way back, he planned in his mind that he would be able to listen to the elegant music of famous actors in a week?

A week passed, but the "Love Listening Gramophone" was still silent and did not come gracefully. Only on this evening did he receive a "proof of trial coupon" book sent by XX Foreign Firm. He opened it and saw that it was written on it: "This is a proof of trial coupon. Each book has eight pages. You can tear it off and give it to your eight relatives and friends. After your relatives and friends have all held the coupon and attached two dollars each, and then asked this firm for this kind of trial coupon, you can give you a Love Listening brand gramophone, record." After he finished reading, he shouted, "Bad luck, bad luck, I've been deceived again."

Commentary

A General Overview of the American Automobile Business in the Last Six Months by Mo-Ya 225

▲ Shanghai's Situation is the Opposite, Everyone is Optimistic

The American automobile trade in the first six months of this year has achieved the lowest results in recent years. However, the situation in Shanghai is exactly the opposite, and automobile dealers are generally very optimistic. Their business conditions are mostly good or satisfactory. The new 1932 models they handle have different lengths of time on the market, but after the Shanghai Battle in February of this year, before the quiet July and August, their business was very strong. Compared with last year, automobile sales in Shanghai have made great progress this year. Although detailed figures are not available at present, according to dealers, except for one exception, all are more profitable than in 1931. This year's new models have many reforms, and British-made cars have also been greatly improved. With both the United States and the United Kingdom making improvements, major automobile dealerships in Shanghai have benefited, and their total sales have increased significantly. In addition, there are also those who attract customers with the lowest-priced cars, which was also not seen last year.

According to automobile dealers in this city, those who had new 1932 models in hand in January of this year achieved excellent business results. At that time, there were few competing varieties, and their strong competitors were slow to arrive, which greatly increased the value of their cars. Therefore, business in the new year increased rapidly, with a sudden surge in momentum. Unfortunately, the Shanghai Battle broke out, and the beautiful hopes were shattered. However, some dealers took this opportunity to sell off old stock and outdated cars that no one cared about. The automobile trade in February, except for military use, came to a complete standstill. In March, after the end of the war, business was extremely sluggish, but it improved slightly at the end of the month, because most Shanghai residents who wanted to buy cars were waiting and watching.

Business in April jumped up, which was a post-war reaction. This upward trend continued until May and June. Sales in June were slightly sluggish, and July was also weak. In August, the automobile business in Shanghai showed a strong trend of recovery, and dealers were encouraged. They were optimistic about the next few months. At that time, there were also some dealers of European cars who, although the cars they represented did not have the special advantages of American-made cars, still had a considerable advantage. This was due to the economy of use, fuel efficiency, and the patriotic enthusiasm of buyers who bought cars made in their own country. For these reasons, cars made in countries other than the United States and mainland China sold well in Shanghai. During this period, the situation in the United States was the opposite of Shanghai. This half-year was the worst period for the automobile business in a long time. In the first six months of this year, the total number of automobile registrations, excluding the state of Georgia, was 655,764 vehicles. This number is still far from the most conservative estimate at the end of 1931. The production of Ford factories was suspended for four months, which experts say was the main reason for the reduction in sales, but it was not the biggest reason for the drop in production. The main reason for the decline was due to the economic recession. To understand the decline in passenger cars in the United States, it is best to compare it with the production volume in 1931. In the first six months of last year, the number of automobile registrations was 1,161,689 vehicles. Comparing the first half of 1932 and 1931, the difference is 505,925 vehicles, a drop of 43.5%.

According to the official statistics received in Shanghai, the number of Chevrolet cars in the first half of 1932 was the highest, with 215,811 vehicles. Chevrolet sales accounted for 32.9% of the total, exceeding Ford, which ranked second, with a quantity of 103,000 vehicles. Ford's percentage was 17.2. Plymouth, known for its floating power, had a total quantity of 62,429 vehicles, accounting for 9.5% of the total. The next ten were Buick, Pontiac, Dodge, Chrysler, Studebaker, DeSoto, and Willys-Overland. General Motors Corporation still ranked first in terms of the largest number of classifications, with a total of 307,016 vehicles in six models. Chrysler Motors ranked second, with a quantity of 116,075 vehicles (exceeding 13,554 vehicles last year, ranking third). Ford Lincoln ranked third, with a total of 114,475 vehicles. Studebaker, Pierce-Arrow, and Rockne ranked fourth (ranking sixth last year), with 27,656 registrations. The same period last year was 30,388 vehicles. Except for Chrysler, this category accounted for a higher percentage in 1931. The total number of other categories is as follows: Hudson-Essex 21,841 vehicles; Willys-Overland 16,528 vehicles; Auburn Cord 7,106 vehicles.

If we compare the number of registrations of individual vehicles, then Plymouth and DeSoto were the most numerous in the first half of this year. Therefore, in fact, Chrysler was the only category that grew, with an excess of 42,657 vehicles. DeSoto increased by 1,382 vehicles. The number of registrations in June was 47,537 vehicles, an increase of 13.6% compared to May, but a decrease of 26.1% compared to June 1931. This was the best month of the year, due to the increase in Ford production by 29,595 vehicles compared to May. If we count the entire industry, there was only an increase of 17,696 vehicles. The number of Ford registrations in June was 52,795 vehicles, the most among all kinds of cars. Except for the states of Arkansas, Maryland, Mississippi, Montana, and the Dakotas, Ford ranked first in all states. In the above-mentioned states, Chevrolet had a slight advantage. The percentage of Ford's total in June was 35.8, while Chevrolet was 24.9. In May, Ford accounted for 17.9% of the total, while Chevrolet accounted for 30%. This reversal was entirely due to the launch of the Ford V8 car, so June reached its peak. Chevrolet had the most in April, with 44,880 vehicles.

The number of Plymouth registrations in June was 16,618 vehicles (accounting for 11.3% of the total). It ranked third in the United States and various states (except for Georgia, which is unknown). Pontiac had 5,026 vehicles (accounting for 3.4% of the total). It ranked fourth in the country. Others only ranked fourth in 22 states. The other cars that ranked fourth in various states included Buick in 16 states, Dodge and Rockne in 3 states each, Nash and DeSoto in 2 states each, and Auburn and Essex in 1 state each. This is the list after the top ten. Outside of Ford, there were only two types that increased from May to June. One was Auburn, which increased by 1,500 vehicles, accounting for 21.5%. The second was Willys-Overland, which increased by about 22%. Ford's increase of 29,600 vehicles compared to May accounted for about 127.2%. Plymouth was the only car that increased in June of this year compared to last year, with an increase of 12,750 vehicles, accounting for about 330%. The number of registrations in June increased in 34 states, including the District of Columbia. Pennsylvania increased by 3,100, California 2,700, Michigan 2,400, New Jersey 3,000, Ohio and Texas 1,100. Although New York was still the leader among the states, the number of registrations was 340 less than in May. Illinois was 101 less. Other states that fell included Kansas, Minnesota, North Carolina, and Tennessee. The number of automobile registrations in Michigan, Oklahoma, Washington, and Washington each increased in June compared to the same period last year. However, the total increase in these four states was only about 1,500 vehicles.
